**Selected Words of Rev. Sun Myung Moon**  
**Rev. Sun Myung Moon's Words Compilation Committee**  

**Preface**  
**President of the World Peace Unification Family, Hwang Seon Jo**

1)  
**Our Time**  
<Prayer> Loving Father, today is November 8th, the second Sabbath of this month. May your infinite love, mercy, and grace be with the children gathered here this morning. I earnestly wish for your guiding hand to be with the countless children across the nation who long for this place, admire you, and offer their prayers towards heaven.  
May the earnestness of the central purpose reach the many children in the local areas, allowing them to always have the motivation and opportunities to connect with the new world.  
Father, please take charge of all our matters this month within your providence. We know well that we have a mission to jointly fulfill the eternal purpose with you.  
Father, although this nation does not cooperate with our intentions, we are aware that our responsibility for this nation remains. Even if no one helps or acknowledges us, may we be your sons and daughters who fight firmly, thanking you for the purpose you have left behind.  
Father, as we enter this time, your children across the nation have set the period from the 10th for a new revival before your will, so please allow this time to be a period of joy before you. This period must become an important opportunity for them to conclude the year 1970 successfully.  
We do not wish for our path of suffering to disappear in sorrow, but we acknowledge that we are entering a time filled with new hope and purpose under your protection and love. As we reflect on this, we earnestly wish for this period to be significant, allowing us to resolve our past sorrows and establish a strong connection in a place close to heaven.  
Father, we have a collective responsibility to march forward with a new banner centered around the many children in Seoul, so please protect us. The Christian denominations surrounding us should be loyal to you and your will, yet they are trying to obstruct our path in every way. However, we must remember that your will remains for us to advance towards the peak of victory, and we ask for your permission to repay you with all gratitude and loyalty. No matter how much they may block the path of heaven, we know that heaven will surely prepare the ground for victory.  
To achieve this, we, as a small group of the Unification Church, must always remember that in comparison to the many denominations and the countless people calling upon your name and following your will, we must be higher and fuller in sincerity, heart, and zeal.  
Today, we must recognize that we cannot remain as just one individual. We must be your children who can be praised as the sons and daughters of the high and noble Father, representing the whole.  
Knowing how important the end of 1970 is, we have much to do from now on. Father, may all our actions during this period contribute to your will and lay the groundwork for your global foundation. We firmly believe that this must happen during this period, and we earnestly wish for alignment between our upper and lower selves to fulfill only your will.  
Your beloved children have gathered here. Reflecting on the past when we struggled to walk this unique path, we must critically examine where the center of our current selves resides and whether it aligns with our hopes for tomorrow. We must seek a new direction and be those sons and daughters you desire, who can inherit the hopes of tomorrow.  
Please allow your heart to dwell in their hearts, and may their lives not stray from the life you oversee. May their life journey be sufficient to inherit your hopeful will, and may you always guide them inwardly and outwardly to align with your desired purpose.  
Let us be your sons and daughters who feel shame even while being loyal to the purpose you left behind, and who can forget their own efforts, so that we may be remembered and praised before you. Father, we earnestly wish for this.  
Father, we are preparing various events this month, so please preside over them personally. May all our endeavors align with your will and become a foundation of glory, allowing this month to be a time of joy in 1970 that you can take pride in.  
At this time, please bless your children scattered across the nation and praise the many children around the world within your will. Protect them. Guide them. We earnestly ask that they may become your sons and daughters who can run tirelessly and unwaveringly until they reach the peak of final victory.  
May your holiness be present in every place where your name is gathered today, and may your merciful hand be with us. We earnestly ask that we may be your sons and daughters who can ultimately be established and praised before you. We offer this prayer in the name of the True Parents. Amen.  
<Words> We know that the times of birth, marriage, and death are significant moments in a person's life.  
**Three Important Phases in Human Life**  
For an individual to be born, grow, and bear fruit, they must establish relative connections, and then they must inevitably walk the final path. This is also true for a nation. A nation must have a founding period, followed by a period of prosperity. After this prosperity, it must inevitably go through a period akin to evening.  
The period akin to evening must be a crucial time when any culture or nation can reorganize everything and seek a new beginning. During this time, it must prepare all the necessary elements to become a new seed, a new factor of life for the future. This time can be seen as a harvest season, similar to autumn.  
In our lives today, there are such days and such periods. In our daily work, morning is a time for preparation, and daytime is for working. Evening is the time to wrap up all the work and prepare for the next day.  
Just as individuals and our daily lives go through such processes, the Unification Church is no different. The Unification Church itself has a period of revival. In this period, it must possess the vitality to overcome all the conditions of its environment; otherwise, it cannot remain as a living entity before that environment.  
Once it has remained as a living entity, it must always be prepared to inherit the fruits of new life, along with the contents related to that life. Otherwise, no matter how much the time of fruition comes, it cannot bear fruit on its own.  
Therefore, it must overcome its environment after being born. Moreover, it must inherit all the conditions that can lead to future fruition and possess the self-power that can motivate the contents of that fruition. Only then can it remain as a fruit-bearing entity needed in the new historical process or in human society.  
**To Remain as a Fruit-Bearing Entity**  
When we think about this, a person must overcome their environment after being born. However, overcoming it is not the end; they must go through a process that allows them to inherit new life and the contents of fruition in the future. After going through this process, they must occupy a rightful position where they can demonstrate effectiveness. For example, just as seeds are sown, sprout, grow, bear fruit, and are harvested by the owner's hand to be stored in a granary, they must go through a process where they are needed for a certain purpose to be harvested.  
The same is true when we look at the Unification Church today. When the Unification Church embarks on a new mission with a new providence, there is content that the providence has, but there are many opposing conditions compared to the welcoming conditions it should have. Therefore, to exist as a new entity in different environments, it must go through a merciless process of struggle. Through this struggle, it must remain from the individual to the family, tribe, nation, and world.  
For such fruition to remain as a single fruit for a nation, it must overcome all trials that oppose and challenge the vitality of the nation. Furthermore, if this is a new path that can lead not only to the nation but also to the world, it must possess the self-power to overcome the environment of that world. However, this alone does not solve everything. Even while overcoming difficult environments, if it does not retain the contents of future hopes within itself, it cannot inherit the hopes of the future.  
Therefore, the internal conditions necessary to inherit the contents of hope for the future become even more critical than the trials of reality. Even if we have fought and won against the environment, we should not rejoice; instead, we must reinforce the contents that we can inherit in the future through this struggle. How to reinforce this becomes the most significant issue.  
Thus, rather than rejoicing because we have gone through a process, we must ensure that the determination made in that process serves as a stimulus for inheriting the hopes of tomorrow and that we stand in a position that contributes to that. If we cannot stand in such a position, we will not be able to become a fruit-bearing entity that can be harvested in front of human history in the place of future hopes.  
**Prepare the Factors to Inherit a New Era**  
From this perspective, what kind of time is the 1970s? From this point on, we are in a time of passing through trials. We have all overcome the trials up to now. When we look at ourselves in this light, we must not forget that rather than rejoicing in the fact that we have overcome trials, the more significant issue is to reinforce the contents of fruition that we must prepare immediately.  
Because this content is an important factor in inheriting future hopes, whether we possess this factor or not will determine whether we can welcome the 1970s as a time of harvest and fruition.  
This period is a crucial turning point that each of us must resolve. If you do not possess the factors to inherit such things, no matter how much the 1970s may help our intentions and allow our church to develop, you cannot welcome that time as your own.  
Looking at the 1970s, we have gone through many events. Through numerous international events conducted repeatedly, we have been seeking and proposing new solutions to society. We are planning various events in November as well.  
Through this entire process, no matter how many events we have held, they must be connected to the future's content and serve as opportunities that can motivate and factor into future development. If we do not become individuals who can invest our efforts into that, even if the 1970s approaches as our time of fruition and harvest, it will become a meaningless time. We must always think about these issues.  
Therefore, this time is a good time for us to inherit and bear fruit in the new era that is coming. To do this, we must have the contents that can bear fruit within ourselves. Those who do not possess a living environment filled with continuous joy, excitement, and vitality must recognize that now is the time to make new resolutions.  
When we realize that we are in such a position, can we rely solely on internal factors? No. We must connect internal factors with external factors. We must necessarily link them with external positions. If our will is not only the will of the Unification Church but also the will of Korea and the world, we must maintain internal factors and connect them with the external environment.  
Now is different from the past, where we struggled against opposition while pioneering our environment. Now is the time to present what we have prepared and be evaluated for its value. This is our position as we enter the time of harvest and fruition. Therefore, we must be evaluated here. We must make comparisons. Which is true, and which is excellent?
and that we must be evaluated on which is more valuable.  
In order to receive such evaluations, we must hold various events in the 1970s. Of course, events that can adapt to national fields are important, but we must also hold events that can evaluate us in Asia. Moreover, we need to carry out global events as well. Why must we do this? Because when comparing our organization with others, there must be aspects that are undeniably superior to those of other organizations.  
From a value perspective, when we are evaluated as something that no one can carelessly assess, the global meaning here will be automatically connected through a single center. This is how we see it.  
What kind of fruit will you become?  
Therefore, here, you must solidify the internal factors that can inherit such hope and aspiration within yourselves, and you must not forget that you are in a position where you must adapt to the external environment based on that solidified internal factor. This must be revealed from an offensive position, not a defensive one.  
When you look at a persimmon tree, flowers bloom in the spring. Persimmon flowers are not particularly colorful like other flowers. The color of the persimmon flower is similar to that of the leaves. So, at first glance, it is hard to tell whether there are flowers or not. Even when the fruit is formed, if it is covered by leaves, it is difficult to tell whether there is fruit or not. The leaves are so lush that you cannot feel whether there is fruit or not. This changes as summer passes and autumn begins; the color starts to change. When it becomes fully ripe, everything inside and outside turns red. Even if the leaves fall, the fruit will remain shining brightly.  
Here, the fully ripened fruit itself can serve as the evaluation standard for the entire environment. We know that there is no one who would not be pleased to see that fruit. The Unification Church is the same. If we consider the Unification Church itself, and if the 1970s are truly a time of bearing fruit, then all factors like leaves must completely disappear. The question is whether we can become like the fruit of a persimmon tree, which bears fruit with a value of fruition on a bare branch.  
Such fruit does not need advertising. Anyone can evaluate the inherent value of that fruit, which is equipped both inside and outside, at one hundred percent. To achieve this, how much has that persimmon tree fought steadily throughout the year? How much effort has it gone through to reach the point of bearing fruit?  
Among the countless flowers that bloom from many branches, the fruit itself has fought harder and made more effort than any other flower's fruit to become a better, fully ripened fruit. It has overcome various harsh environments, such as winds and rains during summer and the lack of nutrients that could cause the fruit to drop in immature conditions.  
If that tree does not bear many fruits and only has one fruit left, that fruit represents the entire essence of that tree, embodying its comprehensive content and external fighting power. Only such fruit can remain. If there is only one fruit left on the tree, that one fruit can substitute for the value of that tree. If it is a persimmon tree, then that one persimmon can establish its own worth, dignity, and authority when autumn arrives.  
How pitiful and sad would it be for a tree that had many flowers and fruits but ended up with nothing but bare branches in autumn, having borne no fruit? However, even if it did not bear many fruits, if it had one fully ripened fruit that could not be compared to any other tree's fruit, that one fruit could proudly boast in front of thousands and tens of thousands of fruits.  
Our time  
There are many religions in contemporary society. Among Christians, there are many denominations. In this reality, if we focus on the Unification Church, which has entered the era of bearing fruit, what kind of fruit does God require from us? As mentioned earlier, many fruits should be borne on one tree, but if only one fruit remains, and if that fruit is a perfect fruit that the tree cannot produce beyond that, then that tree can establish its value, authority, and dignity through that fruit.  
In the same way, if we liken the Unification Church to a tree, it must bear fruit. The Unification Church has gone through many storms and trials since its inception, moving toward a single fruit. Here, what kind of fruit that fruit itself will be is a significant issue.  
To become a glorious fruit,  
From this perspective, you must critically examine whether you have truly welcomed a normal spring, a normal summer, and whether you can become a fully ripened fruit in a normal autumn.  
When looking at that one fruit, there are branches, leaves, roots, and seeds. To say that the fruit has been harvested is to say that the entire tree has been taken. Moreover, because that fruit has many seeds, it stands in a position where it can have dozens or even hundreds of trees centered around that fruit.  
The fruit of one tree represents that tree, and whether ten years or twenty years have passed, it must inherit all the vital factors that the tree wanted to pass on through its historical experiences. Only then can it be harvested as a complete fruit.  
And during the process of the fruit's growth, that factor must not be severed even once. It must be allowed to grow continuously. From the day life begins until the fruit is harvested, passes through the owner's hands, and is stored in the warehouse, that factor must not be cut off at any time. Whether it is windy or even during a storm, or any trial, that factor must not be severed. It must be consistently retained and held within itself.  
From this perspective, when you enter the path of faith, you will feel the emergence of your new life, joy, and new hope. You will make a resolution that "I will become such a tree, such a person, and such an existence before the world." From the day you make that resolution, all internal factors preparing for that hope and autumn harvest must remain unbroken. As time goes on, you must continue to affirm and add to that. Without this process, you will not see the fully ripened fruit.  
The 1970s are our time. So what does our time mean? Is it a time to fight, or is it a time to reap the harvest? Everyone hopes for a time of harvest rather than a time of struggle. People fight not just to struggle but to win and receive glory. In other words, the reason for fighting and wanting to win is to seek glory; if there is no glory in winning, there is no need to fight. That glory is possible when the results of victory in the struggle are achieved. Everything works this way.  
Then, when we look at the 1970s, what does it mean for the Unification Church? It is a time to reap the harvest. In reaping the harvest, will we focus on the members belonging to the Unification Church, or will we only reap the fruits we like? Or will we reap the fruits that the Republic of Korea likes, or the fruits that the world likes? The positions are all different.  
The more God loves us, the more He will not want the fruits to be harvested solely as values within our church. He will want them to be harvested in a way that the nation looks up to and the world looks up to. Therefore, the question is whether we have consistently carried the factors that can lead to such fruitful harvests.  
Where will we reap the highest and best fruits that God desires?  
If we have consistently carried the factors of fruition, where should we bear fruit? Should we bury ourselves in the church to bear fruit? What kind of environment and foundation do we want to establish for that fruition? Is it God's wish and our wish to bear fruit within the church? No one would want to see the fruit harvested solely within the church. If we think this way, wouldn't God feel the same?  
The more valuable the fruit is, the more it will be desired to be harvested in front of the most honorable beings at the highest level. When we consider this issue, the scope and position are broad, great, high, and precious. Therefore, it is everyone's hope and desire that the Lord of heaven and earth, God, would want it to be harvested as something more precious in front of the world.  
When we consider this issue, today, no one would look at the fruit solely as the fruit of the Unification Church. Anyone who values it in the Unification Church can value it even more in the nation, and the world can value it even more than the nation. Ultimately, the fruit should be something that God, the Lord of heaven and earth, values even more than the world.  
Then, what is the highest and best position that can be valued more than the world, more than the nation, and more than our church? When we stand in that highest position, it becomes a historical fruit.  
Because there were no such fruits in the past, when such fruits emerge today, that one fruit harvested today will illuminate the past. Moreover, by harvesting that fruit, we can extend the hope for the future once again.  
Because we have brought such fruits this year, will we not bring such fruits to future generations? Centered around the value of the fruit to be harvested, will we not look forward to the hope for the future? When we consider these issues, we can say that the present is our time of harvest. The time of harvest refers to the value of fully ripened fruit, and that value must not be harvested solely as a value within the Unification Church.  
So where should we plant the value of this fruit, and where should we reap it? We must reap it in the nation and in the world. To reveal the fruit as more valuable and to have it recognized and evaluated as more valuable, we must pioneer an environment that can shine centered around the nation. Because we must shine this before the world, we must establish connections with the world.  
In the future, our church's events and movements must not end with the rituals of the Unification Church but must reveal a form of fruition that all people can admire more than any national or global rituals. If our church is the one responsible for the providence of restoration before the world, then how our church reveals that will be the direction we must head toward in the future. You must understand that this will not happen suddenly or start suddenly. It must be carried out based on the continuous content of motivation.  
All these events should not just flow by; they must become part of us and become a factor in the second environment, gradually spreading wider. The factors that have become personal must be connected as factors of the church, the factors of the church must be connected as factors of the nation, and the factors of the nation must be connected as factors of the world. When this heads toward complete fruition, a new cultural world will be established.  
When we think about these issues, we must now become such a valuable fruit. We must become a fruit that can be evaluated within the church. In other words, you must establish yourselves as beings who can be evaluated. You must become autonomous beings. This is the issue.  
You cannot suddenly come into the harvest season, having done nothing usually, and say that you will not lose to others. A fully ripened fruit must be trained and its content must be complete even before it blooms. At the same time, it must be matured through trials during the process. If you remain in a position of avoiding difficulties, you will fall again when faced with such trials. You must stand in a direct position, face the trials, and remain steadfast. At the same time, you must cultivate your inner strength and be strong in the factors necessary for fruition. It must not end merely with absorption; you must also become a being who can defend yourself with external resistance to bring forth fruit.  
You must be excellent in every aspect to become the seeds that the owner can use.  
When we consider this, what position are you in at this moment? When you see yourselves as individuals of the Unification Church and say, "Ah, I am a follower," such people will not be harvested by an excellent owner. They will never be harvested by the owner who seeks the best seeds. Such people will rather be eliminated. To stand before the one owner who is looking for that one true value, you cannot be a follower. You must be excellent in every aspect. You must be well-equipped in all respects, both inside and outside.  
Some people may be good at church life but not at social life. Others may be good at social life but not at church life. In this regard, those who are good at social life but not at church life lack the factors and content necessary to bear the fruit mentioned earlier. When comparing who is better between those who are good at church life and those who are good at social life, those who are good at church life are better. Those who have the factors of fruition can move forward with hope for tomorrow, but those who do not have the factors of fruition cannot establish a relationship with fruition.  
To bear fruit, you must have consistent environmental factors. It is not something that is harvested spontaneously. It does not happen just because you suddenly show loyalty. From this perspective, those who prioritize solidifying their inner life over their external life are better than those who can boast about their external life. Therefore, you must be equipped with the factors of complete fruition both inside and outside.  
Those who can absorb and integrate all external environments centered around such internal factors and reveal an inseparable value in their lives will develop. Such people will have friends both inside and outside the church, so they will not feel lonely. People engaged in faith often feel lonely. This is because they feel a deficiency in their inner life, which leads to feelings of loneliness. They may also feel lonely due to deficiencies in their external life. Without completely reinforcing these two areas, no matter how much you try to have new hope for the future, you cannot have it. Isn't that so?  
That is why our young people should say, "Ah, I need to study. I need to understand the will of the Unification Church."
This is good. I must cultivate my skills to realize this meaning. Then, what will I do with the cultivated skills? I am preparing for external life. No matter how much I have developed my skills, if I do not have the internal content to carry and urge those skills to develop into external relationships, those skills will not be realized. No matter how much skill one possesses, if the inside and outside are not aligned, it will not work. The stronger the internal content that can develop into relationships, the more realization can be achieved. The broader and larger this scope is, the more it will grow. This is a natural principle.

From this perspective, we must feel that our time is gradually approaching. In the past, a significant wave was created in society centered around our church. Moreover, a major issue has arisen in the established church community. The established church community is feeling threatened and fearful upon seeing the development of our Unification Church. As a result, the top officials of the established churches are now in a frenzy, trying to devise some countermeasures. You should not look at this environment and feel pleased. You must have the self-power to absorb this environment as your nutrient. You need to have the internal factors that can digest it.

It is crucial not to just float aimlessly in the air. This is more important than anything else.

The past and present must be certain for the future to be certain.
When someone who does not know about the Unification Church asks, "What is the Unification Church?" what will you say? Will you say that the church with the sign saying "Unification Church" in Cheongpadong is the Unification Church? The question "What is the Unification Church?" implies a desire to know not only the past and present of the Unification Church but also its future. Therefore, when explaining the Unification Church, you must start with its history. You should answer, "The Unification Church was started by someone at a certain time, went through this and that process, is currently like this, and will be like this in the future." This is the kind of answer that is being sought. Asking "What is the Unification Church?" is not asking what a Unification Church member is. The question itself carries a historical significance, meaning it encompasses the past, present, and future.

Thus, how should we assess whether the Republic of Korea is a nation with hope for the future or not? The issue is not whether they are doing well in the present. The issue is what kind of historical process they have gone through. The current state that has gone through a historical process leads to the conclusion that the future will be like this. In other words, the past and present must be certain for predictions about the future to be made.

So, what about our Unification Church itself? The Unification Church has its own history. That history intersects with other histories, pulling each other. If two people pull on a rope, one side is bound to break. So, which side will break? The side that is neglected will break. The weak side will break. Here, one is the historical tether, and the other is the modern tether. If both are strong, no matter how much they pull, they will not break. Everything is like that. All beginnings, processes, and ends are like that, and motivations, content, and results are always like that.

Now, regarding the history of our Unification Church, can we maintain our current state without breaking, no matter what historical forces we pull and tug against? Do you have the self-confidence to strongly assert history and the present age? Are you a possessor of beliefs that are stronger than the ideologies and traditions of modern times? If you have that, you will endure.

Therefore, in your faith life, you should not think, "I attend the Unification Church just because I have to go to church." You need a belief that says, "I go to church to glorify history and adorn this age." You should think, "My attendance at church is a result of history that can shine. It is to adorn the present age. It cannot be done without me." You need that autonomy. When you go out, even if someone opposes you, you should have the belief that says, "Let's see who is right, you or me. I will definitely bring about better results than you."

You should think about the women who have faced opposition from their husbands and suffered from their children. This will inevitably require more opposition and suffering for some time. You have neglected your family while following the purpose until now. However, that does not mean you have neglected your family. At some point, you will be in a position to fulfill responsibilities that no one else can fulfill in your family.

You have come out following the purpose because you were in a position where you had to choose between the two. The purpose becomes the content, and the family becomes the external environment, so you must first establish the internal content. You need to set the theoretical principles and then manage the resulting life. In other words, you must establish the content and then manage the results. When the content is established, you should be able to manage that environment when you enter your family.

When we think about our past, present, and future from this perspective, truth is always the fruit of the past. It is the fruit that has been recognized by many people. This becomes the critical standard for all issues, the center of the present, and the starting point for the future. The future begins from truth. This comes first; nothing else comes before it. The starting point of the future begins from truth.

The fruit of a tree is the historical fruit that the tree has borne over the course of a year. It is a historical fruit and, at the same time, a fruit of reality that holds greater value. The higher the value of that fruit, the more one wants to leave it as the starting point for the future. When you seek seeds, no one would choose the worst ones. You would want to choose the best among the precious ones. That is why truth is referred to as the unique starting point for the future.

Therefore, true fruit is the fruit of the past. You must understand that it becomes the center of the present and the standard for the future. The essence of truth does not leave the past; it lives on, does not leave the present; it is attached, and it absorbs the future. Thus, truth becomes a subjective heritage that encompasses the values of the past, present, and future.

Looking at the 6,000 years of restoration providence history, that 6,000 years of history has emerged to find the completion period of restoration providence. Everything is included and alive within that completion period. When this happens, Abraham lives, Moses lives, Jesus lives, and all historical unfinished figures are resurrected here. The very essence that fulfills the value they longed for is the mature fruit. When this happens, that fruit itself can become the source of all life in the present because it is complete. This becomes the standard for critiquing and evaluating the world. From here, the future begins. This is meant to come first, not last.

Therefore, truth remains in the end. The true remains until the end. It not only remains until the end but also starts anew in a new era. Such things do not happen all at once. They must be comprehensive factors that span the three processes from the past through the present to the future. The past must be continuously connected there and remain as a factor that overcomes the environment of the past, remain as a factor of the times, and be able to endure as a factor of the future. This is what constitutes a mature fruit.

When you stand in such a position, God will come to you even if He has to abandon the world. Even if He has to cut down the tree, He will cherish that one fruit. Even if the tree burns and falls, He will want to keep and preserve that seed because He loves that tree.

That is why Jesus said, "What good will it be for someone to gain the whole world, yet forfeit their soul?" (Matthew 16:26). No matter how much one possesses a tree, if it has no mature fruit, what use is that tree? Even if one loses the tree, possessing the fruit of life is more valuable. The tree cannot continue life for future generations, but the fruit can continue life for future generations, making the fruit more valuable. You must understand that Jesus spoke from this perspective.

Therefore, you should view the history that has passed until now as something for you, the current age as something to establish you, and the history that will come as something that begins from you. If there is someone who carries God with this perspective, they cannot help but receive God's love. Of course, the path that person takes will be filled with twists and turns. When you stand at the center, there will be many twists and turns.

The higher the mountain, the more it faces all the winds blowing from all directions. It appears as a central object that encompasses that terrain, so it encounters trials from all sides. You must overcome all those trials. No matter how unpleasant the shape may be, the entity that overcomes those trials will proportionally increase in value the longer the history is. The more lonely that environment is, the more the value corresponding to that loneliness will emerge. When this happens, hope will automatically take root. You must understand that your desire to climb a high mountain also has such meaningful value.

True victors
Our Unification Church must not leave the fruit solely for the Unification Church. What our Unification Church asserts and teaches is, conversely, the opposite. It is to prioritize the tribe over the family. When asking whether to demand the fruit of the family or the fruit of the tribe, one must establish the fruit of the tribe through the family. It demands the nation over the tribe, and it seeks the fruit that can become the center of the nation over the fruit that can become the center of the world. Whether viewed from the perspective of pursuing a mature fruit or from the perspective of demanding valuable content, this is a rightful and proper assertion.

Thus, people are told to live from a public standpoint. A public standpoint means prioritizing the family over the individual and the tribe over the family. This is because the larger field is public. So why should one live like that? It is because one is pursuing a more valuable fruit.

Therefore, centered around 1970, it is said to mobilize the blessed families' wives starting from December 1. If men think, "This time only the wives are being mobilized, so it has nothing to do with me," they become irrelevant to their wives. Mobilizing some wives and mothers means mobilizing them from what standpoint? It represents the family. It not only represents the family but also represents the church. Furthermore, since the Republic of Korea is failing to take responsibility, it represents the Republic of Korea. It represents not only the Republic of Korea but also the world. It represents not only the world but also the spirits of the spirit world and countless ancestors. Therefore, you should feel a sense of fulfillment in this mobilization. It is undoubtedly so.

There are countless families that want to emulate me in the path I take. This is indeed the case. If there is a housewife who has not started as a blessed family in the Unification Church, she will not be able to evade her inner struggles no matter how much she tries to hide them until this period ends. Even if she manages to evade it and claims victory on a national level, if there are those who have achieved victory on a family, tribal, and national level, she cannot step forward first. Isn't that so?

Young people who have just entered the Unification Church say, "Oh, I wish I had joined 10 years ago." Even someone with a university degree and a doctorate laments, "I wish I had joined the Unification Church 10 years ago." Those who joined 10 years ago or those who have only graduated from elementary school envy those individuals.

Therefore, no matter how much one claims victory on a national standard, one who has achieved victory on a tribal level cannot be compared. Similarly, no matter how much one has achieved victories on both the national and tribal levels, they cannot compare to someone who has also achieved victory on the family level. Furthermore, no matter how much one has achieved victory on the family level, they cannot compare to someone who has achieved victory on the tribal level.

The results may be the same, but the more extended the history, the more complex the content becomes. Thus, even if victories appear from the same standpoint as history lengthens, the weight of that value cannot be compared.

From this perspective, when comparing someone who graduated from university and vows to serve the church a thousandfold with someone who has only graduated from elementary school but has steadily paved the way since the founding of the church, which person is more precious? It goes without saying that it is not the university graduate but the person who has only graduated from elementary school who is more precious.

Our Unification Church members must transcend the idea of moving for the church. Of course, this purpose is the church's purpose, but to establish this as the purpose of all humanity, we must first establish the church's purpose as the purpose of the nation. Only then can the nation be restored, right? The purpose of the nation must be established as the purpose of the world. Only then can the world be restored, and the purpose of the world must be established as the purpose of heaven for heaven to be restored. After that, we must be able to uphold that purpose as the purpose of God's love. When that happens, it will be the time to fulfill the purpose.

What time is it now?
In this sense, our time is in a transitional period. Until now, we have sought the time of fruition. When will that time of fruition be? Fruition does not happen in the past or the future; it happens only in the present. Today, this reality is the time when we can find fruition.

This time is the time that many people who sought the time of fruition in the historical age have longed for. This time is the time that the prophets and sages have longed for, and it is the time that God has desired throughout the 6,000 years of providential history. It is also the time that this age desires at its center.

Whose time is this? It is our time. It is our time, and it is not only our time but also the time of the nation, the world, and heaven. The fruition that can be harvested at this time is not limited to my own self but holds the value of the universe. Even if the most challenging environmental factors confront that self, it cannot be denied. When this happens, it can become the source of life with a new seed in the face of the global environment.
Therefore, no matter where you are placed in the wilderness of Africa, you must be able to apply this. Even if you enter a mountain alone without anyone supervising you, and even if you befriend the animals and birds within, you must apply this in front of them. It is not a matter of whether someone is watching or not. Whether it is the essential color of the fruit or its authority, even if you do not know it, you must become that which cannot not go. 

This fruit does not change color based on who is watching. At night, it may appear dark because there is no light, but when light shines upon it, it is always a blue fruit. Therefore, this time we call our time must possess the comprehensive value of the historical era. 

If you are not able to be that fruit, you should at least be someone who can protect that fruit. Even if I cannot be the fruit, I can be someone who protects and watches over that fruit. If you cannot be the fruit yourself, you must establish a relationship with the fruit. So how do you establish that relationship? You must become someone who can watch over, protect, and supervise the fruit by the owner's command. If you cannot become the fruit, you must at least be such a person. Only then can you receive even an indirect qualification to participate in the glory of the fruit based on what you have observed about that fruit. Those who cannot do even this should at least know where the fruit is and go to see it. Then, you are better than those who have not seen it. 

So what kind of person will you become? Will you be the fruit, the observer, or the spectator? 

The established church has had issues with our Unification Church since the past, but in the past, they looked down on us as something trivial. However, now they feel a sense of intimidation. Now, you must mobilize your entire life and your utmost circumstances to prepare. 

Recently, Professor Seo Nam-dong commented that there is no revolutionary content or political content in the Unification Church. When considering this, we should present something new rather than fighting with our fists. We should propose something new that is not from the past. 

Because we present something new, it is not yellow. It is not yellow; it is red. The essence of it can be understood when you observe it. For this reason, we are currently undergoing a silent revolution. 

The significance of three years of mobilization evangelism 
What should we do at this critical point? We must hold hands with one another. When it is said that the fruit that can be borne here is on the eastern branch of the tree, it cannot be said, "I only need the sap from the eastern branch" if that fruit is to represent the tree. For the fruit of the eastern branch to represent the tree, it must suck up the sap from the western, southern, northern branches, and all the way from the top to the roots. 

What does this mean? It means that you must become a single connected entity. Each of you is an element that reinforces the life force of the fruit. It is absolutely necessary. Without standing in a position where you can be recognized for respecting such an absolute relationship, you cannot expect mature fruit. 

In this sense, how do you evaluate the value of your family members? Since it is certain that you will receive cooperation from them to become mature fruit that has more value than your own life, the whole must unite horizontally. You must become a combined entity, standing in a slightly prominent position and developing around that. 

From the day after tomorrow, we will hold a revival meeting. Who has been designated to give the lecture this time? "I have been designated." You need to give a lecture, but you also need to create an environment for the lecture. 

In the autumn season, everything that is not needed for the fruit will fall off. However, if all the leaves were to fall off at once along with the first leaves, the fruit of that tree could not ripen. The leaves must fall one by one so that the sap that was going to them can gather in the fruit. In this way, as the leaves fall and fall, the fruit ripens. 

Our Unification Church is the same. Looking at the Unification Church, we have gone through the autumn season until now. Now we must prepare to welcome spring again. To welcome spring, we must overcome the critical point up to the year 1972. Whether the fruit has become a life-bearing seed or not can only be known after passing through the harsh winter season. This life must confront that evil winter and engage in a struggle of "Am I strong? Are you strong?" If you are pushed out in this struggle, you die. We are fighting from this position now. 

Yesterday, when I went to Sutak-ri, someone came and asked, "They are telling us to leave all the children at home and mobilize. What should we do?" I replied, "How would I know? You all know better what to do." You know better how to proceed. The path I must take is not the one I am currently on. I have already passed the path I must take. There were times of tribulation and storms on the path I took, but they are all behind me. 

Now you must become seeds and be planted to welcome the spring season. To become fruit, you must organize all the surrounding environment, right? A fruit hanging on a bare tree is not trivial. It is not trivial that something is hanging there. If you do not want to be attached there, then you should not become fruit. You must plant something pure. 

In a family, you must take the most precious thing and plant it. The most precious thing in a family is neither the father nor the children. The most precious thing in a family is the mother. That is why we mobilized the mothers. However, if someone comes out and says, "Oh, my husband is like this, and my children are like that..." such a person will surely fall. 

In the 1960s, we focused on individual fruit, but in the 1970s, we must achieve familial fruit. What has been God's wish in the providence of restoration until now? While individual fruit could be seen during the time of Jesus, familial fruit could not be seen. That is why He desires familial fruit that can overcome the cosmic misfortunes of the universe and can also bear the difficult crosses of the family. This is a matter of the women in the family. However, it cannot be a woman who can only remain in the family. She must be a woman who can remain in the family for the sake of the nation. A woman who can represent not only the nation but also the world and heaven and earth can become a daughter of God and receive God's love. This is an unavoidable fact. 

Until now, history has not been based on horizontal standards. Now is the time to go out centered on the family. Here, all sorts of things will unfold. You must understand this and consider whether you will be registered in heaven as the family blessed by the teacher during this period. When registering, neither the husband nor the wife should register alone. Both the husband and wife must register together. The Unification Church still does not have a household registration. A household registration requires sovereignty. Therefore, you are pitiful people. That is why the teacher is mercilessly pushing towards the path to establish a household registration. This is legitimate guidance. 

The three-year period to bear familial fruit 
If you do not do this in your generation, you will be passing it on to dozens or thousands of generations. Will you sacrifice such a long historical era, or will you sacrifice a short era? Sacrificing a short era is the legitimate way of guidance. That is why the offering always comes from sacrificing the present. To prepare for all future long-term sacrifices, conditional offerings are established and sacrificed in the present. God has established this as a valid principle. 

Our time is not a time created by the Unification Church. It is the time that history has brought forth, the time when God's providence can be established, the time when the Republic of Korea can gather all the history it has endured through its unfortunate history, the time when it can raise a new banner of hope amidst the despairing history of humanity, the time when it can become the fruit of all past things, the time when it can be the center of the era, the time when it can raise the banner of the future. Such a time is laid before us. Do you understand? 

Where will this be determined? It will be determined based on the world as a foundation, centered on a nation, a tribe, and established on the family. Therefore, there cannot be a providence of restoration that excludes the family. There can be a providence of restoration that excludes the individual, but there cannot be a providence of restoration that excludes the family. 

Then someone may ask, "Where is the providence of restoration that excludes the individual?" If Noah's family, for example, had Noah the grandfather not betrayed God for 120 years and had not made mistakes, but had died in the middle, what would have happened? At that time, it would have been centered on Noah's family to gather things up. His sons could have continued the lineage. That is why the providence of restoration is centered on the family. Only with a family foundation can successors emerge; one cannot do it alone. One cannot carry on the lineage alone. Who succeeded Jesus? No one did. 

The meaning of the providence of restoration is to establish a family-centered foundation of providence in any era. It is not the individual that is central, but the family. The individual is necessary to seek the family and go through the vertical process of indemnity. That is why we must start vertically centered on the family. It is because the woman, Eve, destroyed this vertical start that elevating women is a principled view. 

In this way, children must go to their mothers, and husbands must go to their wives to be restored. Because that wife is working hard for the nation, the husband must also love the nation and establish a mindset that loves both the children and the nation in the process of indemnity to be newly restored as a family. That is why the 1970s is the time for families to be established. You must understand that our time is approaching. 

What is the main idea of the 66 books of the Old and New Testaments? It is to prepare the family that God desires through Jesus and the Holy Spirit. You stand in a position of fruit that can inherit that family from a horizontal foundation and fulfill it on behalf of it. This is the resurrection body of Jesus and the resurrection body of the Holy Spirit, laying the foundation for the heavenly family to meet in reality. 

Therefore, there must be an absolute process through which families must go through a new principle and law from the 1970s to the 1972 three-year period. You must understand that now is the time for familial fruit. Do you understand? That is why our time is not the time for individual fruit but the time for familial fruit. The family is the center of the past, present, and future. 

Then, who must establish the self-power and autonomy to discern in front of the world of Satan in the family? It must be your wives, your women. That is why we are mobilizing the women. For that reason, the teacher of the Unification Church is merciless. 

Let us step forward vigorously towards the new spring. 
What would happen if we told a mother about to give birth, "If it is hard, just bear with it"? It would kill both the mother and the baby. Even if it is hard and painful, you must shout, "Push harder! You must push harder!" During childbirth, the person who shouts mercilessly to push harder with wide-open eyes is the one who truly loves. That is how it should be. If it is not like that, then it is a killer. That is why now is the time when the teacher takes the most merciless position towards you. 

I also have a family and children, and if I mobilize the wives this time, our children will be at home, and there will be those who will send the blessed children to orphanages, and there will be children who will lose their mothers and search for them. All sorts of bizarre situations will unfold. Would the teacher of the Unification Church not feel a pang of conscience? Do you think I have not thought about such things? 

What is the teacher's position from a principled perspective? I have experienced all these things. The teacher has tried to do it voluntarily rather than being commanded to do it. From the time of pregnancy, preparations were made to settle things. However, someone who has crossed a critical point and comes back to the flat ground is a crazy person. Do you understand what I mean? Since the teacher has gone that way, you must go that way too. 

Now the teacher must establish a position and must not avoid this paradoxical method of making you suffer. Are there people who misunderstand that? Those who misunderstand that are bad people. It must be done this way so that you can cross over the mountains and follow the teacher. The teacher makes you suffer, but I feel a sense of responsibility to prepare everything to give a place to those who have suffered for several years. Do you understand what I mean? "Yes." 

If I do not take this responsibility and tell you to do this, I would not be able to lift my face before heaven. The teacher is not such an unprincipled person. It is because I am a conscientious man that I do this. Until now, I have not stepped into an external position because I cannot represent the Unification Church with the teacher's prestige when the family has not been established. That is why I try not to appear in public as much as possible. 

It is a good opportunity to speak to a large crowd and to promote the Unification Church. Even during this wedding ceremony, if I were to speak for an hour and a half, I could certainly convince those who came and make them interested in the Unification Church. Our Unification Church members shed tears and plead to meet one person, but why did the teacher let the numerous crowds just flow by? Is there nothing to say to them? Of course, there is, but I cannot do everything myself and cannot speak to them. If I make a big noise without establishing a foundation for my own children, it would only bring shame before heaven. In the future, the teacher will build a church and establish your positions before stepping into public. 

In that sense, our time, this time of ours, is not a time that just flowed in the 1970s. It is a time that has been woven through an official process. This is the time when it will come to an end like a cliff. It is not a time that extends but a time that returns. That time is also the end of the world situation. We must be able to bid farewell to the last time and enter into the historical, pitiful critical point of the winter solstice, forever parting and welcoming the new spring to make a joyful start. We must become women of significance who can step forward vigorously, one step at a time, at this boundary line. 

You must not have a pitiful attitude of being dragged along, shedding tears and snot. I do not want to see that. We must meet this time with significance. The question of how you resolve this will be of interest regarding the families blessed by the teacher. I will watch quietly. 

Our time only comes once. 
Now that you understand, let us tighten our belts and run for just three more years. What will happen after that? Whether it flourishes or fails, the Unification Church will become evident and will appear on the horizon.
You are destined to either rise or fall; it will not simply end as it is.  
So, in this historic transitional era, the time you can have, that path is not a different one. It is the path you can remain on. Isn’t that so?  
The pendulum must go up or down along the beam; it cannot deviate from that. There is no other way to go. If you cannot go during this period, you will have to lament throughout your life. There is nothing more pitiful than being excluded from the axis.  
Let me tell you a story from the retreat at Yamok. There was a reservoir with a possibility of danger, and it looked frightening because of the thorns. The sharp thorns were poisonous, and even a slight prick would cause everything to fester. Everyone, regardless of gender, went in to catch fish, and the teacher led everyone in.  
However, some people said, “Oh, how can we go in there? What if we catch a cold?” So, I said, “Do as you please.” That person is still remembered today. I won’t mention their name. If you ask that person if they remember the events at Yamok, they would say they wish those times would come again. But the time has already passed. Even if you were to do it ten times or a hundred times, it wouldn’t be the same. The real thing is one. It is not two. No matter how confident someone was, when the Yamok retreat is mentioned, their conscience makes them feel ashamed. Conscience is truly good and wonderful. They know what is shameful. That is the shameful salvation.  
When a person who used to sneak away while their parents were suffering sits in a place where they are honored as a filial child, is there any hell worse than that? It feels like everyone looking at them is cursing them.  
The spirit world is like this. No one tells you to go or not to go. Even among the blessed families of the Unification Church, various forms will emerge. Yet, no one tells you to come or not to come. Moreover, among the women, there may be those who think, “I wish the men would suffer a bit… Why does the restoration providence make it hard for women?” But we must restore through the center of women.  
When you look at the women of the Unification Church, some are well-dressed, but many are exhausted and have no choice but to follow along. How many will remain if we continue like this? If no one is left, the teacher is prepared to do it again, even if it means bringing forth the mother. It is not that I am placing my hopes on you.  
Because this time has come, you must center yourselves on the will and manage all internal factors inside and outside. With strong conviction, you can push through the external environment and have the self-power to push through the nation and the world. If you resolve to embark anew and stand in a fruitful position at this time, you will know that you can stand proud before heaven, and I hope each of you will resolve to do so.  
Then, while women are doing this, are men just spectators? Men also need to strive so that women do not become exhausted. If there are men who only take naps while women are working hard through the night, they will be struck by lightning. A man should love his country more than a woman and love the will more than a woman.  
Even if a man is apart from a woman, he must establish the dignity of heaven. The subject is a man, so he must take responsibility to transform and guide all the foundations of women. This is the position of men. In this sense, I ask you to regard the fruitful time of the 1970s as a time when you can shine.

You have known in places we do not, and you have labored in places we do not labor. When we are not sad, lonely, or suffering, you have endured sadness, loneliness, and pain. Yet, while watching over our path to death, you have promised the day of resurrection. We, the ungrateful children who do not know this fact, come before you once again. In every way we look or think, the more we examine everything, the more we feel we are still in the form of sinners, and we must realize that we cannot present ourselves before you as we are.  
Father, please let us realize once again how great the mission we must fulfill in this 1970s is. Our time is not something found through our own lives today, but it is something that you have fought for, watching over the historical crossroads that have flowed from the day humanity fell until now. We are those who have been found through the foundation of your hard work, which has taken place countless times whenever our ancestors betrayed you. We must sincerely thank you for this grace.

However, as the nation and society enter a chaotic environment, we realize that we cannot trust in the nation or the world, but only in you, Father. The more we know this, the more we must strive to become captives who can be seized by your profound will and heart. If there had been no sad history in the Unification Church, even if it had become a global religion, I know that it would have had to leave behind a process of trials to establish any new providential connection in the world. The time is approaching to testify to the living appearance of your sons and daughters, so please do not let us become sons and daughters who lose the authority and dignity of heaven. As we pledge to fulfill our duties of loyalty and filial piety before you, may we become a group that swears before you in every place that we will become individuals who can inherit the worldly fortunes of the 1970s.  
Even if we lose our nation, we must not lose you. Even if we lose our people and our families, we must not lose your will and your inheritance.
