On the morning of November 15, 1970 (Sunday), at the Headquarters Church.

We thank the Father, who is so gracious, on behalf of the entire universe. When I think about whether I have truly become someone who can call You Father with a heart that pierces to the bone, I realize that we have not truly recognized or appreciated the hardships You have endured to pave the way for us. Father, every time I discover my shameful self, burdened with such debts, I find it hard to look up to heaven, and even when I look down to the earth, I must recognize my sinful state that feels shame. This is the pitiful situation of us, Your fallen descendants, who have caused You to toil until now, and I earnestly hope that this time will allow us to realize that.

Deep within our hearts, we must recognize that even at this time, the cry of life is moving forward together with You, in connection with the continuous history. Therefore, our conscience always urges us to go for good from the heavenly side, and every time opposing evil appears, it bears witness to us that heaven is confronting it. We must truly repent before the Father for our past actions, where we acted without knowing fear in front of the voice of conscience and the direction it moves.

Father, please dwell deeply in our hearts as we earnestly plead at this time. Grant us a strong heart to abandon everything and follow towards the world You command and desire, and may we become individuals who can discover ourselves while simultaneously following in Your footsteps towards a new world.

Father, You have never forgotten the standard of how Your beloved son and daughter should be, and You have followed countless humanity without ever forgetting it. Also, when we think of You guiding many followers towards that standard of desire, we come to understand that the path You walk is one of unimaginable suffering, a path of disgrace, and a path of painful restoration. 

While we often think centered on ourselves, we must now resolve to sympathize with the pitiful situation of the Father, who must save not only individuals but also families, societies, nations, and the world.

When we consider that what You long for in this world is the nation You desire, the people You wish for, the family You yearn for, and the countless humanity You seek, we feel Your heart that wishes to embrace all of humanity as if they were the citizens of one nation. We must long for the families You seek beyond individuals, and beyond families, we must long for tribes, nations, and the world. We must again resolve at this time to become individuals who can emulate Your holy figure and heart, pursuing the standard of longing.

We must not become like lifeless stones, lamenting our own pitifulness without realizing it. If we have emotions and feelings in our hearts, we must become sons and daughters who can recognize and appreciate the amazing content with which You have come. Even in times of hardship, we must realize that we are not alone, but that You are also sharing in the loneliness. When we experience sorrow, we must feel that we are not the only ones who are sad, but that You are also grieving with us. Even when we find ourselves in unjust and painful situations, we must recognize that we are not the only ones there, but that You are also present. This is the heart that those who walk the path of filial piety should feel, and it is the heart that a son seeking the position of a filial son should possess.

That is why we emphasize the faith of empathy. We must experience daily that You are alive through emotional processes, and I earnestly hope and wish that You will allow us to feel this once again at this time.

Now we must lay ourselves bare before the Father. When I say, "This is the person of my heart, this is the person of my body, this is the person I desire," I must ensure that the person of my heart, the person of my body, and the person I desire become one in the Trinity and resemble the image of the Father. I must become a representative who can substitute for the essence of the Father. However, when I discover how far I am from the image of the Father, the greater the gap, the greater my self-reproach should be, and my heart of self-criticism should grow.

How much have we lived opposing heaven and opposing goodness with such a self? Moreover, when we think that we can still be that way from today onward, we feel that we are traitors before the Father and a group that adds sorrow before Him. Father, this time must be one where we resolve anew not to follow in the footsteps of such enemies.

Father, quietly knock on our hearts and open the doors of our hearts. We must become humble sons and daughters who bow before You, wishing to discuss justice and the affairs of heaven in the midst of Your gentle guidance. We must hope for the holy time that You will seek beyond our own shortcomings. Since You are the Father who has come to this sinful world, You cannot help but bear the burden of sin, and since You are the Father who leads sinful individuals, You cannot bear the atonement for sin alone. We must feel that You are a pitiful Father. Before such a Father, we must not become those who add to the burden of the cross, even if we cannot show filial piety.

Knowing that the Father is in such a position, when we think about how many sons and daughters there are on this earth who can forget themselves and step forward, declaring that they will take responsibility for all these difficulties, we must feel once again that this is a pitiful land and a wretched earth. Because of this world, You have drawn the image of sons and daughters who can communicate with Your inner feelings, and You have come seeking the new family that those sons and daughters must unite to establish, and we must feel that You have come to create a new nation centered around that family. Therefore, we must recognize that You have established this Unification Church.

Father! Now You must become the center of everything. You must be the center of our desires, the center of our living environments, and the center of my personal life and character. We must become humble lambs who can follow behind the Father who works so hard. No matter what path of hardship You may ask us to walk, we must rather thank You even more for the grace with which You protect us in the midst of gentleness, and when we think that You are waiting for sons and daughters who can risk death to overcome blocked environments, the more we realize that there are no such sons and daughters, the more we must feel how painful and lamentable that is.

Now, longing for that day when we can once again be embraced in the Father’s bosom as naked beings, we must return to being like children who can forget everything, longing for You and thanking You while receiving the ties of life from Your loving heart. We ask that You manifest here at this time and embrace us as the beloved sons and daughters You have longed for. In that moment when You caress us with Your merciful face and loving hands, may we become sons and daughters who can be embraced in the love where You lament over history for us, desire for the present, and bless us to grow in the future.

May we become sons and daughters who have such a bond with the Father’s love that You cannot leave us behind. We have gathered here to grow in that way and to become Your sons and daughters who can weave such hearts and build connections. We must not move along with the worldly people who flow with the passing time. What is it that we, who have come out here this morning, long for and desire? It is not any worldly wealth or value. The only desire of all of us is to be embraced in the realm of Your love, so please come and hold our hearts and bodies tightly and lead us. May this be a holy time where we can feel Your high and precious heart of love, I earnestly hope and wish.

The word God must not become a distant word to us. The word Father must not become a word that flows by without forming a bond with us. We must know that those who have a Father who pierces to the bone, who can be served in the place aligned with the one thought of our wishes, who can be present in conversation as a living Lord, and who can be an unforgettable object of admiration in our lives are blessed. 

Those who pursue such a path will remain even if the earth perishes, and the Father will hold such people and share Your story, so I earnestly hope and wish that there will be many such sons and daughters on this earth.

The more this world becomes evil, the more we must realize that all the circumstances of heaven are gradually cooling down and that Your will is becoming increasingly distant. We must become captives seized by one heart for Your will, forgetting everything. Without that, we cannot become people who can uphold the dignity and face of the Father on this rugged earth, so I earnestly hope and wish that there will be many sons and daughters who feel this.

This morning, please remember Your children scattered throughout South Korea. May they become sons and daughters who, even after dedicating their bodies to fulfill the way of loyalty and filial piety before You, still feel insufficient. May they not become sons and daughters who add to the burden of the cross before the suffering appearance of the Father, I earnestly hope and wish.

We must not become sons and daughters who seek to receive the Father’s love while placing conditions on it. We must be sons and daughters who can run to You with fervent hearts, forgetting all circumstances, wanting to give everything and share in Your joy, and we must be able to welcome You with raised hands, with a heart that exceeds that of any parent. We must become Your children who know that only with such a heart of admiration and such expressions of longing can we walk the path of restoration.

Father, how much have You labored to lead the Unification Church until this day? More than having anything to boast about ourselves, we must become Your sons and daughters who can hold onto Your garment from a deep place and hear Your greater and more wonderful circumstances. Please make us humble sons and daughters who can wish for Your commands. We must not become ungrateful children who send the Father away in sorrow. We must not become descendants who follow in the footsteps of such ancestors, so please have mercy on us as we seek the new path of unification today.

Father! When we lay ourselves down here with all our sincerity, may this place where we bow down become a precious place that we can never forget in our lives, and may this place where we plead before You become a precious place that we can only experience once in our lives. As humble sons and daughters who await Your holy command, who can present nothing before You and rely solely on You, may this time be one where we discover ourselves who can return completely to Your side, I earnestly hope and wish.

Today, we know very well that we cannot rely solely on our own appearances. I earnestly ask and wish that You will give us a new form that can align with Your heart and Your will, even if it requires a new whip.

Please bind together the children of unification scattered throughout South Korea with their longing for the Father. At the same time as pursuing the noble value of loving the Father, may they be connected with a heart of admiration, realizing that they must meet and cooperate with one another. May only the Father be angry, and may only the Father be the center, so that we can have the appearance of sons and daughters overflowing with joy, placing the Father in the spring garden, and may we become the objects of the Father’s comfort on this desert-like land. I earnestly hope and wish for this. 

Knowing that there is a purpose in the Father’s labor to make the group of unification into such a group, please have mercy on Your children who are responsible for this church and protect the path they must take.

Now, I earnestly ask that You make us Your sons and daughters who receive the new words You command, equipped with a new day and a new self, and actively take on the new mission toward the new heaven and earth, and I pray all these words in the name of the True Parents. Amen.

<Words> We know very well that the world we live in cannot be a world of goodness. Even when looking at individuals, we can feel that individuals are not the foundation of peace in their lives. In other words, we discover that the direction our hearts wish to go and the direction our bodies wish to go are different.

In other words, my individual self is not unified, and the foundation of opposing good and evil is writhing within me. This situation is the same for the environment in which we live. We cannot pursue any resting place or factors of happiness on our own. Because my individual self is like this, the society I live in is like this, the nation is like this, and the world is like this. As a result, this world is one where there are good people, but there must also be evil people who oppose them.
We know well that we have become a world filled with evil.
A world divided and opposed by good and evil.
Humans originally seek to avoid evil and pursue good. Our hearts are always striving to establish a good world and eliminate an evil one, yet on the other hand, we can feel strongly that within ourselves, evil thoughts are powerfully acting against good thoughts. The more we bring forth a strong good heart, the more we realize that evil hearts are always in opposition to it.
Moreover, even when the good heart moves towards a certain goal, it is difficult to clearly understand that goal, and in the process of moving towards that world, it is hard to find processes or connections that can stimulate the good heart. In contrast, evil is filled with such processes and is connected all the way through. 
When we look at this, those who have a heart that seeks truth inevitably find themselves in a position of living a lonely and sorrowful life. 
We must recognize that the path of those who carry forth goodness is not a smooth one. When an individual pursuing a unique character of goodness tries to choose their environment, we realize that there are not many who welcome that individual on this earth. When we see that a good individual does not receive support in drawing a good family, we will feel that the path before the good family, which aims to create a good lineage, is surrounded by increasingly difficult evil conditions.
Furthermore, if a good lineage aims to create a good nation, it is certain that tremendous evil forces will rise up against it, trying to block the path of that lineage. If there is a good nation that seeks a good world, it is certain that because this world cannot become a good world, evil nations will not cooperate with the path of that good nation but will oppose it in every way.
For this reason, throughout history, there have been saints and wise individuals who have come and gone, and no one has received welcome from their times and environments for advocating any claims for goodness. We know that whenever an individual makes such claims, many others have opposed them throughout history. We must understand that when a family seeking goodness emerges, many families have fought against it.
In front of a good lineage trying to walk a certain path, many evil lineages have risen up to fight against it, and if humanity inevitably demands a good nation, that nation has not been welcomed by all nations but has faced total opposition. The struggle between good and evil nations cannot be resolved without a decisive battle over whether good will remain or evil will remain, and we know well that this historical process of struggle has occurred.
To fulfill God's wishes, 
From this perspective, what would God's wish be? It must be to establish one world that transcends nations. If it is God's will that one world must be realized on this earth, there must be countless peoples who can inherit that one nation, and there must be countless families that can constitute those peoples, and there must be individuals who can form those families.
Therefore, if there is an individual who can completely inherit the one world that God desires, how sorrowful must be the path of destiny that individual must walk? Or if there is such a family, how great must be the trials that family must face? If there is such a lineage, how great must be the struggles that lineage must endure? When we think about the path that such a nation must walk, that nation cannot bear all trials from its own individual perspective alone; it must become a nation with a national character that can take responsibility and confront global evil to inherit the world.
When we consider this, pursuing the heavenly kingdom is the path of religion, and establishing God's will is the standard of living for religious people. The question is, how many religious individuals are preparing with such inner content in their daily lives to have the character necessary to inherit such a nation by confronting evil? Although God requires such individuals, when we think about the fact that there are none on this earth, we realize how desolate this world is in front of all the wishes our conscience pursues, as we struggle daily with our bodies to leave traces of our conscience.
Thus, by our individual strength, we cannot do anything. Since we cannot choose with any individual ability or means, what is needed here is the Absolute Being who can solve all problems and become the center of goodness. We must establish a relationship with the Absolute Being as the one who governs a nation of future generations, rather than as the Absolute Being centered on my individual reality, and we must establish an absolute connection. Without this, we cannot push through this wicked environment and wicked world. When we look at such issues, the relationship between God and myself must have a strong and absolute connection that cannot be severed by anyone, without going through a third connection. Without this, no matter how much we pursue an idealistic world, we cannot meet the world we desire. This is only natural.
For this reason, God tells humanity, “Believe. Believe absolutely!” It is not about believing based on any circumstances or conditions, but to believe absolutely. If one believes through any circumstances, they cannot become an individual who upholds the will of the nation that God desires. If one is swayed by their environment and believes based on what they think they know, such content cannot be the basis for inheriting an absolute nation. Such things are of no value, and that is why today, the realm of faith demands absolute faith from humanity.
From the perspective of absolute faith, relative factors cannot be permitted. The term relative only exists after an absolute standard has been established. Without the absolute being determined, the noun relative cannot be used. Therefore, unless one has a standard of heart and blood that can push through even when the world is swirling around, one cannot confront evil. 
Knowing this, God demands absolute faith from us humans.
When absolute faith is firmly established, what will God command? He will require absolute action. That is why the saying that nothing is impossible for those who believe comes from this expectation of action. One must act with the conviction that their actions are not just their own, but are actions united with God, and only then can they bring about a new creation.
Everything in this fallen world is not a new creation. It is what God created long ago, but has been corrupted and tainted by the invasion of Satan, demanding resurrection. Therefore, without the content and origin that can be recreated, one cannot achieve the resurrection of their own individual self, the resurrection of their family, or the resurrection of the tribes, nations, and states needed in heaven.
One must become a self who can pursue a definite result through absolute faith and absolute action to establish a relationship with God. Otherwise, they remain in the realm of Satan, and absolute goodness cannot establish a relationship with them. You must understand this.
Humans must discern between good and evil.
In a world where good and evil are opposed, an individual is not simply born as a son or daughter of the Kim family. We have fallen into a place where good and evil are separated. Here, our hearts and bodies are divided, and good and evil are playing a game of attraction. Evil attracts in its own way, and good attracts in its own way. However, when we look at the environment we live in today, we see that we are not living within a realm of good conditions and emotions, but rather in a realm of evil conditions and emotions. We are placed in such a conflicting environment. (The speaker explains while writing on a board) Here, if we set a central position and cross this boundary, we become evil; if we cross this boundary, we become good. You are wandering in this position.
That boundary is drawn between your body and mind. As that boundary expands from the individual, what happens? That boundary always moves forward centered on the individual. Therefore, not only the individual centered on me but also the family centered on me is caught in this struggle. The lineage centered on me is caught in this struggle, the nation centered on me, that is, the Republic of Korea, is also within this realm of struggle. When we look at humanity as a whole, the entire human race is also within this realm of struggle.
From this perspective, it can be said that as the end of this world approaches, the internal and external, spiritual and physical will become increasingly divided. Therefore, the social phenomena of a certain era arise centered on the ideologies or philosophies of that time, and inevitably, individuals, societies, and the world must be woven together from opposing contents that have different origins in their spiritual and physical, or internal and external aspects.
In other words, when we think about ourselves as those who must discern the environment of good and evil within the realm of fallen nature, the path of destiny we must walk must go through this global bifurcation, settle one of the paths, and confidently organize the world. We must understand that without the emergence of such an individual, family, lineage, nation, and world, a new paradise of welfare cannot come to this world.
For this reason, you must understand that today, the two philosophical trends of materialism and idealism are moving this world. The threats to our lives today are due to those philosophical trends and ideologies. The world is similarly threatened by these philosophical trends. You must understand where such origins come from.
To unite with the Absolute Being, evil must be eradicated.
An individual cannot only cling to goodness. It will be resolved globally, and either good will prevail or evil will prevail. When good prevails, one lives; when evil prevails, one perishes. Thus, this world is racing along the path of life and death.
Individuals are historical products. Families are also historical products, as are nations and the world. But how much of the products of history are good? When considering my individual self, how much of it is a product of goodness? What percentage of the good exists in the living environment you are in, and what percentage exists within your individual character?
When we look at whether we have more factors that can connect us to evil or to goodness, the whole is surrounded by factors that can connect to evil.
In the path of evil, education is unnecessary. Anyone can go there without education. Because it is a history that began with evil, anyone can go there without education. Is there a need to educate someone to walk the path of evil? It has become so by itself, which is why today we educate people to discern based on moral ethics and the standards of conscience.
What is the focus of this education? It is centered on goodness and centered on conscience, yet how many people are based on that educational standard? Anyone can do evil without learning. Anyone can achieve a perfect score in that regard.
In such an environment, our conscience always tells us to be good. Our hearts constantly urge us to become good people, yet have we become good? When we consider this issue, today is a lament, tomorrow is a lament, this year is a lament, youth is a lament, middle age is a lament, old age is a lament, and is it not a life that ends in lament? In other words, does it not end in evil? We cannot help but reach this conclusion. Because we have come from evil, many humans who have lived and passed through this world have struggled in evil and are heading towards evil.
When we look at religion today, what is the Unification Church? Is it a place that teaches to become evil? If so, there is no need for the Unification Church. Evil does not need to be taught. It can be done well without teaching the path of evil. The Unification Church rejects this entire evil world because it is evil and teaches the path of goodness that can be taken directly. Who is the subject that teaches the path of goodness? Who must walk that path? It is the Absolute Being of goodness who must walk that path, and it is the path that the Absolute Being of goodness can embody. 
One must walk the path of life and the path of living that can draw such an absolute path of goodness.
What kind of life and what kind of existence must that be? That life must not be one that can be judged through the historical process. The saints and wise individuals of the past did not achieve the world and character they desired. Those who are leaders of religions or those who should be guided by leaders cannot do so. Why? Because we see that they could not achieve that world through the sects they established. A religion that cannot present a deeper content than that cannot inherit the will of hope for the future world.
Therefore, what is the issue for you? It is to completely eradicate evil from the individual. After eradicating it, there must not be any factors that can graft onto evil. One must become a self that can completely distinguish and organize the factors of evil and can become one with the original form of goodness. Only such a self can become one with the Absolute Being of goodness. No matter how much one lives in a hellish world of death, if their conscience becomes one with the subject of absolute goodness and possesses the subjectivity that can encompass the environment through the factors of goodness, the world is being distinguished from that individual.
Therefore, the conclusion is that a religion that affirms the world cannot become an absolute religion in this evil world. Although one must listen well to what is taught at home or school, one must understand that the environment itself cannot be a family or school that can provide decisive judgments and teachings from an absolute origin. That itself is also tainted by the evil world. It has not crossed the boundary. Even if you achieve your purpose, the question remains whether you have crossed the 38th parallel or not. This is the issue. 

Honestly and conscientiously, you often say that you do not feel guilty. You ask if living conscientiously is not enough, but the question is where the limits of that conscience lie. We have individual rights, family rights, tribal rights, and furthermore, national rights, ethnic rights, and global rights that we must live by conscientiously. When you live centered on the conscience you long for to create a unified heaven and earth, it is commendable. However, even if you claim to have lived with a conscience that does not deviate morally among the people living in the Republic of Korea, that conscience does not suffice. When you say you live by a certain belief, you must ask whether that belief can guarantee a unique world beyond the global one, whether it is a belief that the Absolute can recognize, and whether it can guarantee such a worldview, such a national perspective, and such a global perspective. If you can say yes to that, then it is acceptable; if not, that conscience is insufficient.

That is why religion brings forth negation. Negate everything! Negate yourself, negate your family, negate the society you live in, and negate the nation; furthermore, negate the world itself. You must have a decisive ideology that can undoubtedly negate all of this. For that ideology, there must be an ideological background that can appropriately lead you even if you have to die a thousand or ten thousand times.

What time is it now? It is the time to restore the individual. A person is meant to be straightforward. A person who has sinned speaks even in their dreams while sleeping. The pure response of conscience is revealed in words. It is the same when you speak, right? When you feel something and believe that feeling is right, words come out. When you confront the very bottom of that conscience, you become straightforward. You use terms like right-wing and left-wing, but who coined those terms? They are straightforward terms. The left side implies something is wrong. Conscience has a foundation that can traverse human ethics and a foundation that can traverse heavenly ethics. When you reach a serious place, it reveals itself. Therefore, when the law of justice, that is, a completed heavenly ethics emerges, everything presents itself fully, saying, "I am this," in front of that heavenly ethics. If it is good, it reveals itself as good one hundred percent.

Look at what the left does. It is all deception, employing camouflage tactics. What is the main theme in their strategic tactics? It is camouflage tactics. They disguise facts as if they are not what they are. Analyzing the evil foundation reveals that evil appears as if it is not what it is.

A person must be honest. An honest person is a conscientious person. To be honest means to be motivated, and to be conscientious means to make judgments based on results. Therefore, to be honest is to be conscientious. What kind of person is an honest person? Is it someone who conceals themselves and employs a double personality? Is there someone who likes a person who hides themselves and treats them well? Can you genuinely like such a person?

When looking at the relationship of ascending and descending, going up is difficult. Climbing a mountain is hard, right? But going down is easy. Likewise, hitting the zero point is easy. Anyone can hit the zero point. If we agree to hit the zero point, everyone can take first place. But can everyone take first place based on a hundred points? That is why evil people all end up in the depths of hell. This is a very serious issue you must consider.

It is the same when you pray. When you pray, at what level do you pray? The world you live in is here. (Pointing to the board) Then where do you pray from? Some may pray from around here. There may be others who come in here to pray, and there are those who pass through this place and pray with body and mind aligned. This is a place that transcends the realm of time, while this is a place confined by the realm of time. When body and mind unite and enter a realm that transcends time, it becomes the position of "I am God" and "God is me." It is like the front and back houses. There is not much distance; it is a relationship of up and down. If you grasp it internally beyond the boundary line of up and down, you can hold it.

Where can God dwell? It is not in some public space of the world but in a person. Then where in a person will He dwell? That boundary cannot be the physical body of a person. It is the heart of a person. In the depths of a person's heart, connections must be made with the relationships of up and down, front and back, left and right, but because this does not happen, it becomes a problem. 

To establish that connection, opposing contradictions arise. Is a person who says it is fine either way a good person? Such a person will ultimately be fine either way. Is that not so? During the Korean War, those who said it was fine either way, whether they were communists or liberals, ended up dying as they went back and forth. Such people cannot remain. They hate both Satan and God. Why? Because when that person does wrong, Satan enters them and plays the game of making them evil. The foundation of goodness within that person disappears, and they become a house of evil.

However, a person divided left and right cannot become a tool of evil until a certain point is determined. They must cross the boundary line to the left to become a tool of evil. However, those who waver back and forth are always tools of evil. Their entire life becomes evil. That is why, in the end, one must determine between the two. What is judgment? It is determining whether one is evil or good. This is the issue.

You are currently fighting. You are firing your cannons centered on your life. Before facing the world, your body and mind are fighting. How do you make peace with this? In this battle, does the body win or does the mind win? Do you think the body wins or the mind wins? You must become someone who can say, "I will surely win with my mind." A person whose mind wins is on the side of good, while a person whose body wins is on the side of evil.

Then what is the secret that allows the mind to defeat the body on the battlefield where body and mind are fighting? Or what is the secret that allows the body to overpower the mind? What is the strategy? This is the issue. The direction through which all weapons and equipment are mobilized determines whether one becomes good or evil. So what is the factor that can resolve this contradiction? This is important. What are the necessary conditions for goodness to be established before humans living in an evil world? What are the necessary conditions for evil to be established? We must understand this and either adopt or eliminate it. These necessary conditions are, upon examination, quite simple.

Before conquering the world, I must conquer myself. 

As a fallen human being, I am an individual connected to the evil world. I was born as an individual, but I want to become a representative of the world. If I were born a woman, I would want to be a global representative of women. You all agree, right? Women, is that true? It surely is, right? Even men, as soon as they reach their teens, want to become the best representatives in the world. Even if their appearance is shabby, they want to be the world's representative in essence. You all agree, right? They want to become global representatives.

Then where does the world come from? The world does not come from me; rather, the world comes from me. In other words, individuals are not born from the world, but the world is formed from individuals. Is that not so? What do you think? Did I come into being because of the world, or did the world come into being because of me? It is from me that the world was born. I am connected to the human ancestor Adam, that is, the ancestor of all. The world was formed from one, from one person; it did not come from many people diminishing into me. Therefore, the world began from me, not the other way around.

Thus, no matter how good the ideal world is, it ultimately begins from me. No matter how evil the world is, it begins from whom? It begins from me. However, the world you live in is already a formed world. It did not start from me, but it is a world that has already been formed. However, if you examine the motivation, it ultimately began from one person. Who is that one person's ancestor? Those who believe in Christianity say it is Adam.

Then what kind of person was Adam? He was a person just like you. He was someone who had to fight between body and mind, just like you. So why did he have to fight? This is the issue. The appearance of today’s me is the result of inheriting his lineage, which has reached thousands of generations. These appearances are connected in the form of horizontal brotherhood, thus forming the world.

So before conquering the world, whom must I conquer? In other words, before conquering the world, whom must I conquer? I must conquer myself. How do I conquer myself? How do I conquer the opposing forces of good and evil within me? This is simple. I must move toward the side of goodness. If I am within the realm of goodness, I will be conquered. I am conquered before this world. (Pointing to the board) You see, right? I am swept into this realm of the world.

What must I do to conquer this world? I must stand in an opposing position. I must stand in a contradictory position. Therefore, I must escape from there. This escape has been carried out throughout the historical process until now. For that, there must be an escape route. That escape route is precisely religion. When you go to work in the morning or anywhere else, you should go with the mindset, “Father, there is nothing on the path I am taking now. <Prayer> Beloved Father, today is November 22, the fourth Sabbath of this month. We know that the time is approaching when everything You have worked for us until now must be revealed. <Words> Everyone hopes that tomorrow will be better than today and that the future will be better than the past. Even when considering yourselves, you would wish that the environment you are in is better than the past and that the present position is better than the future. You would wish for improvements that transcend time and space, reaching to infinity. This is the wish of humanity.

To fulfill that wish, we must not advance aimlessly but must advance with value that can shine infinitely. 

Because humans wish to improve, if there is an absolute being who created humans, that absolute being would also want to shine more brightly in the future than in the present. We can think that while observing us, God would demand an even more brilliant tomorrow than today.

When humanity progresses and faces better results, God will feel joy, but when we find ourselves in a situation where environmental conditions are worse than the present, He will feel sorrow. This is an undeniable fact.

Just as we can analyze a person based on all the circumstances and contents they are connected to, the absolute center, God, cannot be beyond the human condition. 

Therefore, the heart that seeks better value is possessed not only by humans but also by God. When we think that God must pursue worthwhile values, we cannot help but consider how to shape and pioneer a tomorrow that is better than today and a future that is better than now, walking the path of a worthwhile world and a worthwhile life.

However, we must recognize that we cannot pursue a worthwhile self in a state of stagnation. If there is no difference between yesterday's 'me' and today's 'me,' there can be no progress or development. We must stand in a position where we can discover a self that is better than yesterday, better than today, and feel the value of a progressing self. If today is worse than yesterday and tomorrow is worse than today, we cannot escape the fate of stagnation or regression.

Anyone, without exception, wishes to be better than their current self. To be better means to add something to the current state, while to be worse means to lack something compared to the current state. To be better signifies prosperity, while to be worse indicates a position that can lead to downfall. Just as we distinguish between addition and subtraction, and between forward and backward, our lives are also on a path that changes based on whether we lean to the right, to the left, or lean forward or backward.

In this path of life, one cannot lean to the right or lean forward without some force acting upon them. Therefore, if we wish for tomorrow to shine brighter than today, we must add something weighted as a plus. Only from such a position can progress be established, and only then can we overcome the stagnation of the present position and march in a new direction.

To advance means to exercise, and thus energy is consumed within itself. This phenomenon is a natural principle.
For an action to occur, there must necessarily be a consumption of energy. At that time, if the energy that is consumed is used only from the energy that is maintained within itself, it will not be able to move a stationary environment. Therefore, a third force must be introduced. If, through this third force, one can improve upon the current stationary position, the issue arises that one must make an effort on their own. The effort at that time should not be an effort centered around oneself pursuing a purpose, but rather an effort that begins from the perspective of pursuing the purpose of a third point. We cannot help but think that we must start from the point where we can stimulate a new sense of purpose.

First graders in elementary school do not study to remain in the first grade, but study to advance to the second grade, and second graders study to advance to the third grade. Similarly, in our lives, we must stand in a position that considers a better future self than our current self in order to make our current self more fruitful and valuable. If we are in such a living environment, we come to realize that the aspect of advancement can be doubled.

Enthusiasm is necessary before the effort for advancement. Then, when we consider the question of where advancement can begin, it depends on how much the pursuit of the third purpose increases compared to the current stationary state. We must think that this becomes the motivation to transform one's position. Therefore, for humans to develop, they must not remain in the stationary current position but must strive to acquire a new form. Continuous effort is necessary to transform our own selves. And continuous enthusiasm is required. Enthusiasm becomes an issue. Without enthusiasm, one cannot proceed. Above all, enthusiasm must be heightened. For someone who has set a purpose and knows what they must do, what is needed before effort is enthusiasm. Enthusiastic effort is indeed an important factor in transforming the current position. Therefore, we must have enthusiasm. However, that enthusiasm should be autonomous rather than relative.

In that sense, we can see that a person filled with enthusiasm can pursue an infinite world and emerge as a valuable person pursuing the value of a life that can shine. The question of how much one can dominate the environment and how much one can break free from the currently fixed position will manifest itself in you as the enthusiasm that God requires. You must understand that this can shorten the distance to the third purpose that you never even thought of.

Everyone longs for a person with such enthusiasm. A person who wants to proceed with enthusiasm can overcome the increasing risks in their path. However, effort without enthusiasm is likely to be interrupted. Therefore, for those of us who wish to advance, the most necessary thing is how to receive enthusiasm that can sustain continuous advancement. Without enthusiasm, one cannot receive stimulation. Moreover, stimulation without enthusiasm is unnecessary. When we think that strong stimulation is connected by strong enthusiasm, we must seek an enthusiastic environment, enthusiastic individuals, and enthusiastic counterparts.

For us humans pursuing a completed personality and infinite personality, we cannot do without infinite enthusiasm. When we consider ourselves pursuing an infinite personality, it is important to ask whether we can continuously pursue that enthusiasm or whether we are in a position to achieve our goals with such enthusiasm. Without adopting one of these two positions, one cannot pursue a completed personality.

For those of us pursuing God, when we consider faith life, there is always a risk that follows the path of faith. This is because there remains a struggle to resolve this with the environment. If we walk that path with strong conviction, the consumption will occur in proportion to that conviction. When there is no enthusiasm to overcome that consumption, rather than advancing in that environment, one will retreat. To avoid this, one must either have the power to supply such enthusiasm within oneself or connect with God, who serves as the relative source of that enthusiasm, to receive it. Without this, one cannot advance.

To receive the enthusiasm of God, who is the subject of enthusiasm, we must consider whether God is always in a position where such enthusiasm can be felt. Indeed, God must be in such a position. Only then can He lead humans, who are not in that position, toward that path. God is omniscient and omnipotent, and since He is the subject of enthusiasm, He is also the subject of enthusiasm. However, no matter how much God is the subject of enthusiasm, we must understand that we ourselves must be the foundation that can accept enthusiasm.

So, what do we need to receive God's enthusiasm? Since God is pure, we must also be pure. When we pursue the third purpose, we must realize that this purpose is tied to an eternal connection with us. In other words, it exists in a triangular relationship, but it can be within me and can exist with me.

To what extent can we realize the sense of purpose within ourselves? The sensitivity of that realization must become the fuse that can lead us to God, who is the essence of enthusiasm. However, when I am powerless and unable to become the fuse of enthusiasm, I cannot align the relationship between God and myself. In other words, if there is one artery, there must be one vein; if something is given in one place, it must be received in another; and I must be the one who can accept what is given in proportion to what is given.

Then, what is the motivation that can induce enthusiasm? It must be pure. There should be no evil. When something is received, it must be reflected purely as it is. This is the issue. Also, where does that enthusiasm arise? It arises from a pure foundation. Based on that pure foundation, the extent to which we pursue enthusiasm and the extent to which we need it determines its emergence. In other words, the question is how much we long for and admire to present ourselves before the subject of infinite enthusiasm. There must be longing ahead, and earnestness must come first. We must think that there is always a connection between earnestness and enthusiasm.

When we think of God as that subject, we should not only want to see God, meet Him, and be with Him, but also want to receive God's love, live within that love, and conclude our lives within that love. This longing must be earnest, and from this earnest heart, the relationship of God's love with us is established. When we think this way, the question arises of how much we long for God.

How much have we admired and yearned for God? Are we in a position where we can forget all of our current positions and dedicate ourselves entirely to God? In other words, can we become a complete minus before a complete plus? When we enter such a realm as a complete minus facing a complete plus, the complete plus will approach the complete minus. Through the pure path of directness, the complete plus will rush toward the complete minus. There, the minus will create a counteraction that pushes from the rear. In other words, to make the force of directness into a form of stillness, there must be a force opposing the force of directness, which acts to push away the force of directness. Similarly, when the complete plus directly approaches me and I hold the position of a complete minus, will not the direction follow the minus? Thus, through the action of the third force, one will advance from the current position to a progressive state. When we consider that this is an inevitable phenomenon in the action body and the laws of motion, we realize that there is no way to encounter a new enthusiasm without pursuing such a position.

Therefore, we need prayer and sincerity. Prayer is not about stopping or fixing the infinite value of oneself, but rather about seeking continuous advancement from a stationary position. Thus, we aim to pursue the foundation that contributes to the Absolute. This is the place of prayer and the place of sincerity.

The question of how much we have loved and yearned for God becomes significant. We can recognize that the phenomenon of advancement exists only in a position where we are drawn into or pushed into the absolute power. When we think this way, we cannot help but be sincere. To be sincere means to push oneself into a state of nothingness. If God is the complete plus, then we are pushed into the form of a complete minus before that existence. This is what we come to understand.

When a high-pressure zone forms a low-pressure zone, the high pressure that was there moves elsewhere. The high pressure is formed somewhere else due to the low pressure. The more the low pressure grows, the more the high pressure forms elsewhere in proportion. As the low pressure enters a vacuum state, it exerts a pulling action. This is the simultaneous occurrence of emission and absorption. Thus, as absorption and replenishment occur, progressive results appear.

That is why religions teach sacrifice and service. In pursuing the infinite value of life, everyone is in the same position, but to sacrifice and serve is to urge the formation of a low-pressure zone in terms of pressure. When one completely gives oneself in sacrifice and service, it will become a vacuum state like that of low pressure. However, when a vacuum is created, the universe must provide a value proportional to what I had.

We do not need to worry about whether the Absolute, that is, God, exists or not. When we have the environment that can give in a true form, God will surely provide replenishment. That is why we are told to give our hearts, our intentions, and our characters. The command to "love your God with all your heart, with all your soul, and with all your strength" is not directed at God but at us. Then, when this giving reaches its peak, how will the result appear? It will manifest as a force of love before the counterpart. It will appear as an action that can stimulate the counterpart. When such an action reaches God, God's love will come to me.

When we love with all our heart, soul, and strength, nothing will remain. Heart, soul, and sincerity will all be spirit. Then, does this mean to love from the position of spirit? No. When we reach the position of being spirit, we will receive greater love.

When we think of this as the factor of the action of love, the question arises of how much we have longed for God today. If one longs for God centered around their own personality and seeks to fill that perspective, they will inevitably lose their eternal development. They will remain stuck at that limit.

Therefore, we must forget ourselves and pursue the infinite God, being infinitely sincere, infinitely yearning, and infinitely admiring. When we enter a place where such feelings are heightened, the stimulating enthusiasm that comes from God will surely arise. When we act with that enthusiasm, God's love will reach me. This manifests as power and becomes an absolute factor that can break through the environment. A person in such a position will undoubtedly advance and develop. We must recognize that this is the principle by which power persists and the principle by which power acts.

When we consider a car, there is something eternal that supplies the power to run behind the car. The car can run only if the action of giving continues on the side of receiving. When the piston performs a suction action, it creates a vacuum state and receives fuel. Thus, the piston performs a reciprocating motion. Through this action, the engine moves, and through the moving engine, there is new progress filled with enthusiasm.

Our individual selves are the same. It is through enthusiasm that we feel stimulation. For a person, if the second purpose is greater than reality, constant stimulation is essential to achieve that purpose. The outcome of whether that person can fulfill their goal depends on how they can continuously supply this stimulation to maintain themselves.

When we think of this, the question arises of how much we have sacrificed for God on a pure foundation and how much we have admired and yearned for God. The place where I long for God and can forget myself, where I shed tears not because I want to but because I forget my position, is a place that seems unrelated to me but becomes an absolute factor that can shape me.

The divine sense received in the state of no-self is the driving force of development. Humans do not have the consciousness that they want to be born when they are born. They are born through the power of God before consciousness. Therefore, development does not originate from the basis of their own consciousness. The formation of my own valuable self begins in the place where I forget myself, where the active results before consciousness are affirmed. In other words, the motivation for God to exist here before my consciousness becomes the foundation for a better version of myself to be formed.

When we consider this issue, the position of saying, "I prayed to feel this, and I feel it," is a position that cannot transcend the stationary and fixed environment. It is a place where one can forget that they are putting in effort, where even if they shed tears of gratitude while praying, they do not shed tears because they think they are grateful, but rather, the five senses act before they think, allowing them to shed tears. We must be in such a place.

Thus, rather than pursuing a purpose before consciousness, those who discover that the relationship that allows them to pursue a purpose is connected with them will develop.
If a prophet prophesies based on their own consciousness, it cannot exceed their limitations. However, if they base themselves on their own being but allow the infinite source of power to come through their five senses, there is a possibility for new prophecies to emerge. There is no such possibility when one is motivated by oneself. The more one enters the realm of receiving the grace of the infinite God, the weaker the notion of 'I' becomes. One must enter into a state of no-self. If one enters into a state of nothingness and receives the stimulation of a greater power than what they felt from the standpoint of existence, they will feel that a new, creative work of God is continuously occurring there. Only in such a place can one feel strong stimulation and discover a self that is more advanced than the current self.

For this reason, one cannot engage in mystical prayer while being conscious of their surrounding environment. In a place where past impressions remain vividly, no matter how earnestly one prays, they cannot transcend their current environment. One must seek to enter into a state of no-self. At the same time, one must strive to discover their pure self. There, all factors of evil must be eliminated, and only the elements of pure goodness should exist. Everything that exists must be made into factors that can align with the fundamental direction of goodness. It is essential to realize that establishing such a foundation is a crucial factor that those who pray must seek.

Taking an antenna as an example, an antenna does not find and sense the vibrating waves by itself. It senses the waves coming from the surroundings. Similarly, humans, while admiring God's infinite senses, can feel the vibrating sensations when they stand in a perfect position to receive those divine sensations. When one feels such sensations, a phenomenon of vibration occurs. The praying person is in a similar position.

Therefore, you must forget your own position and feel the sensations coming from God like an antenna that can infinitely receive God's senses in a tranquil place. By elevating yourself infinitely, recognizing an infinitely pure, valuable, and meaningful self, when you move toward the boundless realm, you will feel that a third power, which you do not even know, connects with you. It is about seeking to enter such a realm.

To develop, one must settle the past. Thus, if my thoughts up to now were of a selfish nature, I must repent. If my past perceptions linger, I must completely grasp those perceptions and discern whether they are selfish or correct. If they were correct perceptions, I must be able to add them to the present; if they were selfish perceptions, I must seek methods to completely eliminate them. If I cannot add the valuable connections of the past to the present, no matter how good those connections were in the past, they cannot relate to the future I am pursuing.

Moreover, when considering whether the facts perceived from the current standpoint are good or evil, if that consciousness does not contribute to goodness, I must completely repent and, after settling that, only add what can remain as pure and good connections. Only then can it become a progressive factor; it cannot remain as it is.

Regarding the future, one must discern whether their thoughts are pure or impure, good or evil, and only select the good elements from the future they are conscious of to ensure that they can be meaningful and progressive. Without doing so, one cannot pursue better advancement.

Thus, one must fill the past, present, and future with goodness and enter into a place filled with goodness. If one enters such a place, they will be able to experience existing at the center of infinite power. At this time, a new creative work of mystery will manifest.

Why is that? Because if one is infinitely filled with goodness, the center must be God, who is the subject of goodness. If I enter such a place, I will discover that God is present in my heart. Upon discovering this, I must feel that the fullness of goodness is mine to experience a new worldview.

In a place where one is fixated on past consciousness and attached to present consciousness, with a self-conceived future consciousness, one cannot host God. One must be a foundation of goodness that can leave only good consciousness and eliminate all evil factors. For example, if light is projected at a 90-degree angle onto a mirror, it reflects back in the direction from which the light came, allowing the source of the light to feel it. Do you understand? The light coming directly to this 90-degree mirror is repelled.

Light reflects proportionally to the angle of incidence, so when light strikes the mirror at a vertical angle, it reflects back as it is. For this to happen, the mirror must be pure. If any impure part remains, it will not stimulate the source as pure reflected light. When the mirror is perfect, it can stimulate the source with perfectly reflected pure light. Therefore, we must be pure. Then God will be pleased.

The position of pure goodness is essential for our development. However, before pursuing that development, the more pressing issue is how to cultivate purity within oneself. Thus, you need time for prayer and time for sincerity. Sincerity must not be offered casually. One must settle the past. If past consciousness remains, one must consider where that consciousness will lead them. One must critically assess how strongly they stand in the past while being intoxicated by it. One must evaluate whether the past was pure and whether they currently stand in such a position. Additionally, one must critique whether their desired aspirations are pure.

So what is the position of pure goodness? Pure goodness cannot exist when it is for oneself. Goodness does not persist in strengthening oneself. Why does it not persist? Because goodness is the foundation for hosting God. To host God in goodness means to acknowledge God as the master of goodness. The master of goodness is not fallen humanity but God.

Therefore, when viewed from the perspective of goodness, if one seeks goodness to elevate and glorify oneself, it is a position of rebellion against God, not a place to host Him. In such a position, the 'I' is present, and thus God cannot be present at the center of goodness.

Goodness seeks something greater. Even when desiring grace, one should not wish for the grace of personal resurrection but should seek grace that can save the world and more. The more one seeks greater goodness, the more they cannot remain in a position where their consciousness is fixed. One's consciousness itself must become a more valuable position that can move around centered on goodness.

To achieve this, one must sacrifice oneself. One must give oneself completely. Only then can a new pathway for dissemination be formed. When a complete minus arises, one will feel that a complete plus capable of acting upon this minus is already present. Therefore, when you enter the realm of grace, you will not know when God has come. In the presence of God, you must feel that He has already been there. You must acknowledge that God has connections that you cannot reach. God can be present in a place that transcends your consciousness.

Thus, in pursuing goodness, do not fulfill it only within limited boundaries but fulfill it from a position that transcends those boundaries. From there, God establishes an inner position. Although it may not manifest in form and shape, if it were to manifest in form and shape, it would appear as a factor forming an absolute personality. Only then will humanity realize through their consciousness that God is present with them. Such a realm exists. Therefore, we must be pure. How pure must we be? We must be as pure as a flat mirror.

What then is pure crying? Pure crying is the crying that occurs when all cells and nerve organs are in harmony. To be in harmony means to be filled. Crying must have the connection that can be filled with joy. Moreover, when one feels joy, there must also be sadness that can stimulate that joy.

If only joy is stimulated all the time, eventually one will be unable to feel joy. While there is joy, there must also be a sad aspect that can stimulate that joy. The sad aspect can quickly move, and although our consciousness may not feel it well, before the absolute goodness itself, before joy, the sad aspect can be transcended. Just as there is light, there is darkness; where there is a high place, there is a low place. A realm where only joy can be felt is not a joyful realm. When that realm changes direction, it will feel sadness.

The appearance of laughing is similar to that of crying. What is the difference between laughing and crying? Think about it. Some people’s laughter seems just like crying. When you look at facial changes, both laughing and crying can make the eyes smaller and create wrinkles on the face. When you laugh, you reveal the public side; when you cry, you reveal the private side.

When laughing, one reveals the public side. There is an old saying that one should not spit on a smiling face. This means that if one does something bad to a person who is smiling, they will be punished, and those who oppose laughter cannot be forgiven. Not being able to spit on a smiling face means one should not act in such a way. Therefore, laughing is infinitely public.

Then, when considering whether God is laughing or crying, since God is a public being, He should not be crying. He should be laughing. However, He is not always smiling broadly. He should be smiling with fullness, but at any moment, He could burst into laughter, or conversely, experience explosive sadness. That is the kind of being He is.

When one understands God's sad aspect, their own sadness disappears in the face of that sadness, leading to joy. After sadness passes, joy comes. The realm of grace is also like that. Therefore, when repenting, one must reach a state of crying to the point of tears and snot, feeling as if their insides are torn apart and their breath is cut off. After such a crying session, joy comes. Do you understand?

What kind of being is God? He is one who is filled with joy, yet can also have infinite sadness that can erupt, possessing fullness inside and out. Thus, when one enters into that sad aspect and reaches the end, it transforms into joy. Conversely, when one enters into the joyful aspect, the boundary of sadness gradually reveals itself. When these intersect and become one, one will feel explosive satisfaction. Isn't that right? When something hot collides with something cold, what happens? It explodes, right? However, when something hot collides with another hot thing, it does not explode. You must understand that the absolute subject formed in harmony is God.

People want friends who have tears. However, they do not want friends who cry all day long. They want someone who has tears but is also filled with laughter. A person should not always have a frowning face. Even in that, one must be able to discover overflowing joy. Therefore, who is the blessed person? The blessed person is one who can cry with others when they are sad. That is how it is. Blessing comes to a place where one does not want to leave forever. Isn't that so?

What kind of place is the blessed place? Since blessings come to a place where one does not want to leave forever, the place of blessing is likely to be like the relationship of a wealthy person. What parent would say that their child’s sadness has nothing to do with them? No matter how much they resolve to do so, the tears will come first, surpassing that resolved consciousness. This is the heart of a parent.

Then, what is the difference between parental love and a child's love? Parental love is based on a heart that can regret giving wrongly even after giving. However, when a child is dutiful, they become conscious of their duty to their parents. This is the love of a child toward their parents. Do you understand? There is a difference. The child knows that they are being dutiful. They acknowledge it themselves. Therefore, the love of a child is lower than that of a parent. Because it is lower, it needs the love of the parent and demands the parent.

Thus, a person who seeks God, who seeks the infinitely pure foundation, cannot enter that place without tears. If they have committed unforgivable sins, they must think of their past and discover that they deserve any punishment they receive, while simultaneously hating that self. Only after that will the voice of joy come. Therefore, those who pursue pure purposes can go to heaven whether they move forward or backward.

In a good place, whether one moves forward or backward, it is heaven everywhere. Because humanity has lost such a place, they must restore that foundation to achieve eternal progress and development. You must think about this fact.

Therefore, when praying, one must repent of the past and the present. One must be honest. "I was such and such a person in the past. There were times like this and times like that." They must repent. And they must have a heart of gratitude for being established in this place despite being such a sinful person. When reflecting on past wrongs, gratitude must come first, and while self-reproaching, even if there is a harsh whip of God's judgment, one must willingly accept it and have the heart to offer oneself as a sacrifice before God. Only in such a place can one receive God's forgiveness.

Thus, one must be forgiven for the past, forgiven for the present, and guaranteed for the future. If the quantity of past evil is great and the present evil entangles one, true liberation cannot be tasted. To become a self that can govern the past with goodness, the present with goodness, and remain in goodness in the future, one’s desire to govern goodness must be strong.

What must that strength manifest as? It must be centered on a heart of admiration.
they would be beaten. This was the fervor and passion that people had when they first entered the Unification Church. They wanted to be there, feeling an overwhelming desire to attend church. Even if the church doors were closed, many would climb over them to get in. Spending a night in a corner of the church was a wish for them. If they were chased away, they would cry and resist leaving, saying they couldn't go even if they died, climbing over the gates.

This requires a conscious effort to connect with the divine and to engage in prayer with a pure heart. When individuals pray earnestly, they may find themselves in a state where they are not even aware of the content of their prayers. In such moments, it is not the individual praying, but rather God speaking through them. This is the essence of true prayer, where the individual becomes a vessel for divine communication.

In this state, one can experience a transformation, allowing for a deeper connection with God. It is essential to approach prayer with a pure heart, free from selfish desires. Only then can one truly align with the divine will and experience the blessings that come from such a connection.

As individuals strive to embody this spirit of selflessness and dedication, they will find that their lives are enriched and their spiritual journey becomes more profound. In conclusion, the journey of faith is one of continuous growth and renewal. It requires individuals to remain vigilant and committed to their spiritual practices, fostering an environment where divine love can flourish. Through sincere prayer and a willingness to serve others, one can cultivate a life filled with purpose and meaning, ultimately leading to a deeper understanding of God's presence in their lives.
