Also, when you eat rice at church, you can't help but wonder why it tastes so good. It's not like it's enchanted by a goblin; it's the same rice as any other, yet it feels special. Even the spicy kimchi and radish cubes have a three-dimensional flavor. (Laughter) Why does the rice taste good when you eat it at church? It's similar to how the rice cooked with love by your parents tastes good. There is so much longing that even relative existence can bear fruit there, making you feel that something bad is good. And because this is related to me and appears as a relative value, it manifests as something good, and even something that doesn't taste good appears to be delicious.  
It's all a matter of nerve function. Right? Taste is recognized through nerve function. However, the nerve function of heaven is a supernatural action. Because it is in a position to oversee the whole, there is nothing bad there. Experience grace, and the world appears as a palace. Even if you are in a filthy place, it feels like a palace. Even when you see maggots playing, it seems like the world's top dancers are dancing. It really looks that way.  
This cannot be felt with today's human emotions, but because it has the subjectivity of supernatural emotions, it can be felt that way. Therefore, everything seen there appears as an object of joy. Thus, it concludes that there is nothing bad in the spiritual world.  
However, if someone says, "I don't want to go to church; it’s just okay. I wonder who will preach today," and wants to stay home, can they return to the nation? Is it possible? What that person should do is find a nation. God blessed Adam and Eve to govern heaven and earth and to govern something greater than a nation, but they could not go to the place of blessing. Similarly, can you, who have a mission to find a nation, sit at home on Sunday and save the nation? If someone says, "I don't want to go to church; I'd rather stay home," that person will fail. Such people have no way to be saved.  
However, if you think, "Going to church is better than sleeping at home," and come to church to meet friends, you will be stimulated. People need stimulation. They need to feel rebuked through sermons and experience frustration. They need to feel, "That sermon is for me." By receiving such stimulation, they can realize. When you come to church, you receive direct stimulation rather than indirect stimulation. Therefore, going to church is better than staying at home.  
The taste of following heaven's will  
Is there any student who wants to go to school just to study? At first, everyone goes because they can't help it. Especially elementary school students go because they are scared of their parents; are there any kids who go because they want to study? At first, everyone is like that. After going reluctantly, they eventually come to know the taste and go to learn. When that happens, their parents are surprised. When they realize that there is something stimulating in that taste, they start to enjoy studying. That enjoyment, when looked at as a whole, is bad. However, relatively speaking, when they study, they find that the range they can act freely has widened, so they develop a taste for studying. No one likes studying itself. There are people who like to sleep, but there is no one who likes to study from the beginning. They like it because studying broadens the range in which they can act.  
Do you find it enjoyable to believe in the Unification Church? There is probably no enjoyment at all. Dislike is the principle. Dislike is the principle, but if you believe, it gradually changes. Old friends seem small. When you meet a friend who was first in class when you were last, that friend, who once felt like heaven, now seems to be lagging behind after discussing Unification Church ideology. It is because of this taste that one believes in the Unification Church.  
Moreover, when you call God, "Honey!" you feel as if you hear, "Yes, yes." When you realize that even the presidents of the world can only be played with in your hands, you feel good and believe. The same goes for the teacher. The teacher did not do this work because he enjoys being persecuted. He did not do this work because he enjoys being scolded. He has done this work because there is a better taste than the taste of dislike.  
Once you step into the spiritual world, there is a taste that makes you envious of no one, which is why you do this work. Knowing the taste of this meaning, when you strike this world with a club, it shatters into pieces, and you feel the reality of it breaking apart. Can a person always endure unpleasant feelings? You might think that the teacher can do that because he was born strong and healthy, but that's not true. How can you do something you dislike? Try doing it for a year or two. You will die. (Laughter) Even so, it is good, so you endure it; if you feel tired and can't live, do you think you can endure it? After doing this, there is something wonderful that allows you to do this work.  
If you lose money in business, it’s the end, but if you make a profit, it’s not the end. Similarly, the teacher has continued this work for ten, twenty years, and because he has not suffered losses and has made profits, it has not ended. That is why he is still doing this work. Isn’t that right? Everything is just business. (Laughter) When doing business, if the principal is one thousand won, a person who does not invest that one thousand won as their own will live and die because of that one thousand won. Do you understand what I mean? A person who wants to do business must invest that one thousand won. Only then can it return with more profit.  
Similarly, as there is a business aspect to you, a person who is satisfied with the current state and does not invest will fail. Business will not succeed. You must invest the capital you have to make a profit. When you are certain that the future self will benefit more than the current self, you become a speculator, throwing your life into it.  
When you roll a pine cone from the top of a snowy mountain, the snow accumulates and becomes a large rock that can collapse houses. Therefore, if you keep rolling like this pine cone, what belongs to others becomes yours, and what is yours can become someone else's, leading to the thought that the whole exists because of you. When you see that, everything is just business. Who would do this work while suffering losses? Look at the teacher. Does he look like that?  
You may also have times when you are quite tired. When you wander around day and night, there are times when you become intoxicated with fatigue. Just as someone who has never drunk alcohol does not know the taste of being drunk, those who have not experienced fatigue do not understand the taste of being intoxicated with fatigue. When you feel tired in the course of living for a purpose, you realize how close God is in that intoxication. There is a place of such intoxication. It is because there is such a place that you do this work.  
The path of revival  
What happens if someone who has entered the Unification Church stops coming? A person, even if they are a prisoner serving time, must have outings rather than just stay in their cell. Do you understand what I mean? Successful people do not stay at home. They frequently go out. Of course, there are times when they go out and get scolded, or someone follows them with a club to cause trouble, but if better people than themselves come and go at their home, that person is successful. So, what is the way for someone who attends the Unification Church but does not come to church? It is to align with the church. A person who does what the church cannot do, centering on their home, will not fail even if the church fails. This is the way to live.  
However, a person who does not do that and stays cooped up at home is already a failed person. Such a person will forget even what they had. If they received grace worth ten thousand won but cling to it saying, "I have to live on this," will that work? "Oh no, I can't lose even a hundred won..." That kind of mindset is not good. If your heart keeps going that way, you will lose what you have. You will even lose your business capital.  
After about a year, you will find that your capital has run out. At that time, when you look for family, there will be no taste like there was before. Naturally, it will taste bad. A person who used to be liked will now seem like a walking corpse, and when they glance at that person, they will feel bad. So, they do not realize they have changed and say that Unification Church members are fickle. They used to like them, but now they say they are being treated coldly. Not realizing that this is a warning for self-reflection, they sulk and keep belittling Unification Church members, and in the end, they will lose their neck, lose their life, and only their body will remain, claiming they are going to heaven. Where are they going? They will end up failing while living in chaos. There are many such people.  
This is either stagnation or retreat. However, if stagnation lasts long, there will be no usable items. Retreat is a foregone conclusion. Therefore, advancement is necessary. A person must have motivation to live. They must have enthusiasm and stimulate themselves. They should not be in a stagnant position, so the teacher is currently conducting a bomb operation to advance, even if it means hitting with a club. By doing this, they can no longer stay in that position, so they have to pack their bags and wander around, experiencing injustices and being looked down upon. At that time, they will realize, "I was wrong. I have lost that wonderful grace from before," and they will finally try to find that lost place again. From that point, they will begin to seek the path of revival.  
The path of revival begins from a state of sorrow and loneliness, lamenting. "Oh Father, I am about to die now. I have no strength. I have nothing." If you repent with such deep sorrow, you can live. Even if you shed tears and snot, and your clothes are all torn, if you cling to it saying, "Oh, I am dying," a way to live will emerge.  
If you go around so busily that people say, "That person is crazy. They are a day goblin," you can live. Try going around from house to house busily. When grace falls, there is a method that is better and faster than prayer to raise that grace. If you used to go back and forth between two houses and grace falls, try going back and forth between four houses. Go around evangelizing at four houses. The fallen grace will rise again. That method is better than prayer.  
Also, if you were going around four houses, try going around eight houses. Even if your legs hurt, you get scolded, and you get beaten, that is because you did it for others, not for yourself, so you have something to say. At that time, when you pray, you will think, "I used to live only for myself, but now I have been beaten for others, so I have improved." (Laughter) Ultimately, that is all for yourself. That is why everyone needs such stimulation.  
So this time, we are going to send out 36 families and 72 families. These families will settle down, and since it seems that they are just spending time meaninglessly yesterday and today, we decided to send them out this time. I want to go see how they live. There are some people who do not like the Triune God coming. Even if three women gather, a fight breaks out; if ten women gather, a fight will break out, and everyone will fail. (Laughter) This time, the 36 families and 72 families must pack their bags and go out.  
A leading role  
New culture develops through movement. New revolutions always begin by breaking the current position, right? This is always the case. Sometimes the teacher does things that seem absurd to ordinary thinking. That is how strength is replenished. It is not for me but for heaven and earth. You must do the same. Everyone must move forward with a pure perspective while looking at public purposes. When that happens, strength arises, and strength is replenished. When that happens, even if the world turns upside down, if you grab it once, it will fall out. Such strength and such action are behind us. Such people appear different every day. Their feelings are different. That is how a person's heart is.  
That cannot be the case from your current position; therefore, you must do things that can break the stagnant and fixed position. You must not retreat. Therefore, to do such things, you must continue to take special actions. If you pray to find a pure position and then act, your enthusiasm will not cease.  
This morning, when the worship started, only a few people came, but after some time, many came. If you are going to come anyway, why not come early? Why come late? It only takes a little diligence. If you think you will be late, you can just go to bed earlier, right? Can’t you think of that? The time you come early is time dedicated to God, which has a value that cannot be bought even with a fortune. That time is dedicated to God, so coming late means stealing from God. Therefore, you must come on time. Because of that, you can compensate for the time you could not sleep and also establish your face before God. When that happens, you can have a better heart than yesterday and draw closer to heaven, but if you come late, you will be sitting there blinking your eyes during prayer, wondering what the teacher will say. Seeing you sitting like that is pitiful.  
A person who plays a leading role is not calm and gentle; they are enthusiastic. Such a person becomes a leader. You must understand that this is certain. A person who is stagnant will fail. To be stagnant means to marry "lost fortune." Do you understand what I mean?  
When it comes to the question of whether to advance or stagnate, a person who does not have the self-awareness that they are advancing means they are stagnant. They have married a goblin of stagnation. While they are stagnant, as a year or two passes, the providence rises from the individual providential era to the family providential era, the tribal providential era, and the national providential era. Can you keep up with that? And then they say, "I have been in the Unification Church the longest, but my value is not recognized." What value? It is a statement that is transparent. It only smells rotten. Such a person can be left alone. God does not need such a person either.
The teacher still does not think of himself as a Unification Church teacher. He is fighting every day with the same feelings as a new member who has just found the Unification Church. That is why he is still developing. Do you understand? When you make a decision, what are you marrying? "You are marrying a goblin." Where will that person go? To heaven or to hell? Even if you try not to go, you will be dragged to hell.

A person who is active is a person who advances. So when we ask if we have retreated or advanced since joining the Unification Church, what do the ladies here think? "We should think we have advanced." That statement is unavoidable. (Laughter) Have we advanced or retreated? "We have advanced." (Laughter) Everyone, if we talk about trees, a living tree keeps growing. If there is a tree that does not grow while all the other trees are growing, that tree is dying. To be dying means that, over time, it will die. Therefore, the issue is that we must recognize that we are fighting within the realm of destiny that we are moving in.

However, there are some trivial people who blame others and do not come to church. The people from Pyeongan-do and Hamgyeong-do were the ones who had advanced. The Queen of Heart  
Fallen humanity must walk the path of restoration through indemnity. Restoration through indemnity means returning to the state before we lost it. However, there must be a condition of offering sacrifices to return.  
Fallen humanity must walk the path of restoration through indemnity.  
When we look at the fall of our human ancestors, the motive for the fall lies with the archangel, but since the archangel is a spiritual being and we humans are substantial beings, the responsibility must lie with the substantial beings, namely humans. In other words, although the fall occurred in the relationship between substantial beings and spiritual beings, the substantial beings, Adam and Eve, must take responsibility for the fall because they are the center.  
Looking at the path of the fall, it extended from the archangel to Eve and then to Adam through Eve. How must we restore this through indemnity? The fall occurred because the archangel lured Eve from the position of a parent, that is, the position of a father, and through Eve, lured Adam, pushing him into the position of the archangel's own son. Because the fall occurred through this process, in the history of restoration, it is essential to present women in the process of indemnity. This is the principled perspective.  
Our Unification Church was founded in 1954, but until 1960, it was a period of preparation. From then on, it became the path of actual practice. So, what must be done at the forefront of the history of restoration through indemnity? We must seek the way for God and Eve to become one. Only by seeking a place where God and Eve can become one can we stand on a level that matches the standard where Satan and Eve became one.  
So, what must be done to establish the condition of oneness? We must overcome and win against Satan, who hinders us from becoming one. In this regard, the environmental conditions that women possess in the satanic world are their crosses. That is, if they have husbands, the husbands are their crosses, and if they have children, the children are their crosses. The Role of Religion in This Era

Of course, they may consider their new religion as a treasure, but religion itself cannot be a treasure. The most valuable central treasure is not religion or individuals, but families.

That is why, even if they have sacrificed and died, they stand in a position of resurrection. They do not perish. And if that nation has sacrificed for the country, the ideology of that nation will remain as an eternal ideology for that country, and if a country has sacrificed for the world, the ideology of that country will remain as an eternal ideology before many nations of the world. That is why goodness survives even in death.

The Bible says, "Whoever believes in me will live even though they die, and whoever lives by believing in me will never die." What does this mean? It means that a person who lives centered on goodness does not truly die. A person who lives for God does not die.

If an individual dies for the family, the family lives. If that family dies for the tribe, the tribe lives. If the tribe dies for the nation, the nation lives, and if the nation dies for the world, the world lives. This is Unification thought. However, evil is the opposite. It disregards everything and seeks only to live well among ourselves. It is about wanting to live well alone.

No matter how hard God tries to find a homeland, it is useless. A homeland cannot be found without sacrificing the Unification Church. So, how do we sacrifice the Unification Church? Is it by living comfortably centered around the church, encouraging each other, and visiting each other's homes? Some people think it should be like that. However, Unification Church members must spread out, with people from the North coming to the South and those from the South spreading to the North, making the entire Korean Peninsula their active stage.

**The Lasting Religion**

While ordinary Christians may only come and go within the church's fence, we Unification Church members must at least take the Korean Peninsula as our stage. We may be deceived, we may be taken advantage of, and we may feel angry when insulted, but still, we must believe. If we are deceived once, we should forgive that once, and if deceived twice, we should forgive that twice. If we keep forgiving, the deceiver will feel a pang of conscience. Even if they initially had no remorse when deceiving, they will start to feel sorry as they continue to deceive.

You can tell when someone is deceiving you by looking into their eyes. If they keep deceiving, they will eventually be caught. If you forgive them twice, they will confess the truth the third time. Everything in the world works that way. Evil people will flee in distress as if they are being pricked by a skewer when they see someone with their eyes wide open. If they pretend not to notice, they will eventually trip over themselves.

Evil people must be treated this way. That is how they will come to their senses.

Koreans are quite resilient people. I am also very resilient. Throughout my life, I have endured this path and have not yet grown weary. Among those who have come here, there may be no one who can outmatch me in wrestling. I am confident I can take them all down. Regarding Internal Organization and Expansion
Now, once we pass the 31st of this month, this year will be over. At the beginning of the year, we set a tremendous slogan of victorious unification front and have fought until now.

The point where internal organization and expansion become issues
This year has been an important period for laying the foundation of the 1970s and for being able to redeem 6,000 years of history, so there have been many events both inside and outside. And there are various tasks to prepare centered around the 1970s, including the issue of the construction fund for our headquarters church. However, I believe that after this December, we will surpass a certain limit.

When viewed from the perspective of our intentions, we realize that victory is on our side. Even when looking at the facts that are witnessing our movements in the spiritual realm, or observing domestic movements, or viewing the victory ideology based on national standards, we can see that we have reached a certain limit. In this way, all external circumstances have come to a certain point due to God's hard work, but the current issue is that internal organization and expansion are what we need to address.

Looking back at the 1960s, it was a decade in which we engaged in a war of attrition. This was because there was a great barrier placed before us, and it was a fight to break down this barrier. Because we fought with all our intellect and sacrificed ourselves in the 1960s to break down these barriers, by the time we reached the 1970s, these barriers had somewhat crumbled, and we feel as if we are on level ground.

The 1970s is a crucial period where we must solidify our roots by strengthening internal organization rather than merely appearing externally, and we must complete the heavenly mission entrusted to us before this nation and the world. Therefore, you must re-evaluate yourselves based on principles. We must also critically review our activities. We need to review and systematize all the contents of the historical process we have gone through until now.

In order to pledge the final victory that God desires at this present moment, we ourselves are the issue. Therefore, the urgent need for internal reorganization has led us to believe that comprehensive education is necessary this year.

Next year, we will engage in external activities, but not just with a very small number of people; we must mobilize all members to engage in activities to ensure that we do not leave any final limits unbroken.

Let’s mobilize to break through the final limits
As you all know, during this period, blessed women have been fully mobilized. Moreover, this period is seen as a crucial time that determines whether we can break through the final limits by investing all the sincerity and efforts we have put in until now. Therefore, women will be organized into teams of ten and will be dispatched to 120 evangelism sites. They will mobilize from the district headquarters to the regional headquarters and to the area headquarters, and we must secure at least 120,000 elite members of our church by 1972. Considering this, if the current members evangelize just one person each month, we believe we can practically secure more than double the current number.

Until now, our church has not been able to establish relationships with existing churches. To establish such relationships, there must be activities of intermediary organizations. Therefore, we are creating something new that will serve as a bridge with existing churches. In order to move towards the highest standards that God desires, we must inevitably expand by establishing various forms of organizations both internally and externally.

Now, the issue is you yourselves. The question is whether you can become leaders who can lead an organization. Therefore, you must exert your utmost efforts until 1972.

Focusing on the women who are going out to engage in activities, we will push to secure at least 120 regular members in the regional and district headquarters over the next three to four months. Following that, the youth and husbands will also be mobilized. We plan to sequentially mobilize in this way to seek a path to connect with existing churches by 1972.

From the 26th to the 28th of this month, 26 pastors attended our principle lectures at the Academy House for two nights and three days. Pastor Kang Won-yong said that not a single person would respond to our invitation, but about 40 people agreed to come. However, due to the Thanksgiving holiday during this period, the number was reduced to 26.

From this, we can see that the perception of existing churches towards us has changed significantly. We invited them in the name of our association president, and many young pastors attended. This fact indicates that the interest of existing churches in us has grown, and they are now at a point where they must study our principles to understand us better. Therefore, we are considering expanding such activities on a large scale.

And the question is how to solidify the activities of the principle study group. In discovering human resources, we must prioritize activities centered around universities. I have instructed the president of the Japanese principle study group to focus on this aspect as well. We are considering how to secure first and second-year students as members, so that internally they can be armed with the principle ideology and externally with the victory ideology, and how to develop their ability to lecture based on that theory. Therefore, during this period, we will have students give lectures and observe the results and reactions, allowing them to practice repeatedly.

As we see each person gradually increasing, we must help them realize how valuable this is. We must make them feel that being absorbed into our system after graduation is better than going out into society.

Still, the purest group is the university students, so we must ensure that they are equipped with the ability to lecture from their junior and senior years. After honing their skills for about two years, I believe they will have no trouble engaging in external activities. Without seeking such paths, we cannot secure internal human resources.

Support frontline activities with sincerity
Taking this opportunity, we are planning to establish a theological college in Sutaek-ri. The overall issues we are planning are aimed at solidifying internal organization. Until now, we have been conducting sporadic guerrilla tactics, but from now on, we will adopt concentrated tactics to secure a base of operations and will start with that combat readiness. You must know this and put in your sincerity and pray a lot. Of course, it is a path of responsibility that is in accordance with heaven's will, but by your sincere efforts behind the scenes, we can exert our utmost efforts to establish that posture both internally and externally.

You must also strengthen the activity system so that you do not fall behind them in the rear. Along with these activities, the headquarters will organize a revival team. I believe we will know the results roughly after about 40 days. After 40 days, we will form a revival team and connect those who are active in each province horizontally so that they can carry out average activities.

You should know about these overall issues and pray sincerely.

Now, the intention is right before us. Seeing this, I ask you to know that the time of victory is approaching us and to unite and cooperate for about three years both internally and externally.

Father, may the foundation of a family that can become the center of the nation you desire and the center of the world be established through us. We wish to be born and resurrected in your joy. Before you long for us, we must first long for you, and before you love us, we must first love you. Before we confess all our circumstances to you, we must become sons and daughters who know that you already know our circumstances.

Father, do not forsake us, the pitiful ones. We know what it means to be your sons, and we understand what content we must possess as your sons. When we see our past selves, or our current fallen selves, or our shriveled selves, we must realize that we stand in a place where we cannot hide our shame.

When we think about how we can reveal ourselves before your fiery gaze, and how we can be in an environment worthy of your dignity, we become anxious that we might tarnish your holiness or that your purity and nobility might be overshadowed. As we pray in our hearts, "You are infinitely high, infinitely precious, infinitely valuable," we must resolve that even if we were to fail a thousand or ten thousand times, we must not harm your holiness. We come to understand that we need to possess a heart that fears your coming even more today.

Wherever the heart of compassion rests, you operate, and when we think that your heart of mercy is intertwined, we must be infinitely grateful and praise you infinitely before your astonishing and tremendous presence. We must be filled with respect. In that deep, quiet, and pure place, the life force of creation must be connected to your name, lamenting the fallen legacy of misery.

Even in the most extreme conditions where one cannot move due to hunger, we must be more intensely filled with longing for you than in that moment when our consciousness is focused on a single point. Today, among the fallen descendants, all cells must concentrate in one place, and all senses must focus before you, calling you as the highest voice, crying out "Father," and in that cry, we must grasp you and feel your reality along with revolution.

Father, have mercy on us. How ugly and shameful our appearance is today! With all kinds of diseases afflicting us, we call out to you in this pitiful state, and you, who have a blood relationship and a life relationship with us, cannot deny us, so we must sympathize with you, the pitiful Father.

How did we become like this, and how did you come to call us your sons and daughters? As we traverse the path of a thousand years of sorrow, we must realize how miserable, unfair, and pitiful it is to be a son or daughter who can only weep and lament with tears of sadness and sorrow before the Father who wished to embrace the sons and daughters of hope.

Today, Father, who has led this unification movement, you promised to love anyone, no matter who they are, and even if you were to forsake the world, you expressed that you could not forsake us. How sorrowful and painful it is for you, who are so precious and valuable, to come and labor among humans who are lower than the filth of excrement and less than the scum of all creation.

As we think about the path of labor you have walked, tracing the path of value that cannot remain with the flowing waves, we must realize that no matter how long we kneel and bow before you in gratitude, we can never repay your grace.

Father, before loving you, we are humans who are madly in love with ourselves, and before praising your value, we are humans who want to praise our own value. Before boasting of your labor, we are humans who want to boast of our own efforts. Father, now we must return to the heart of a child. We must long solely for your life-giving embrace. We must forget everything and be filled with longing, like a little child yearning for its mother's milk, and receive the pure supply of your love once again. We must inherit the pure heart of your love.

Father, I earnestly ask that you do not forsake us at this time. Please take charge of the Unification Church. The reason your sons and daughters have been despised and ridiculed until now is because they have called upon your name and sought to walk the path of restoration you have left behind, so Father, please remember that at least.

In walking this path, there have been times when we had to forsake our children, times when we had to leave our beloved husbands behind, and times when we had to turn coldly away from our beloved parents as if we did not know them. This was true not only for friends but also for our environments and our countries.

When we think about this, if we, who have lost what we had to exchange for you to Satan, cannot grasp you and establish a connection with you, then we must go back to reclaim what we have lost. If that happens, how much will we be mocked before Satan, and how much will your sorrow be compounded? We must realize that there are pitiful groups who hesitate and struggle over the path of destiny, thinking about this, and we must understand that you are a sorrowful being, you are a troubled and lonely being, and you are a lonely being who cannot plead with anyone on this earth.

Therefore, please allow many to arise who wish to live for you and for you. If you have a greater desire for a small group of unification than for thirty million people, I know that this unification group will never perish. It must not perish. Because the connection with you is so great, because there is a historical value of labor you have shared with us, and because we have a heart that wishes to live for you rather than for ourselves, I earnestly ask that you protect the path of those who desire this.

We see that even trees prepare for the fruit of life when spring comes. We must not become humans who cannot meet the spring season in the path of life. After meeting spring, we must be able to welcome summer. After the lush summer season, we must bloom flowers and gather all the nutrients into a single fruit that cannot be exchanged for anything, possessing a life force that will not be invaded by anything even as the cold winter approaches.

Even in the most rugged and frozen places, we must possess a life force that boasts of its authority and is not captured by anything, so that we can meet spring again in the future and sprout the shoots of life. At this time, we must also become pure beings of life that can sprout the shoots of life upon meeting spring.

As we welcome summer, flowers bloom and fragrances fill the air, and the heavenly hosts come to sing of life and praise the value of life. We must understand that we cannot become a distinct, subjective being without possessing a clear content of life that cannot be exchanged for anything and cannot be broken by anything.

No matter how cold the winds may blow, no matter how icy the icicles may freeze, we must possess an authority that can transcend and melt them, ensuring that we are not threatened by life again, so that we can become the heirs of the hopeful kingdom.

At this time, because you have called us, we have come here. Therefore, please connect us with you. Among the countless beings living on this earth, may your abundant love accompany our steps as we tread the path that others do not think of and that seems dry and uninteresting to others. May your unending heart of hope dwell within the life connections of these individuals. As we pledge to walk the current path for tomorrow, may we offer the value of our fruits before you and become your children who continue to advance.

At this time, we have gathered to engrave your deep and high character and your abundant love that does not tire even in the suffering of history, and to become sons and daughters who can represent you in the current struggle for tomorrow's hope. Therefore, merciful Father, do not leave us behind, and may your high and precious glory be with us.

Thus, may the countless heavenly hosts, as well as our ancestors who have gone before us, the many humans who are yearning for life connections on this earth, and even the descendants who will come in the future, be united through the connection of your children who are bound to you with longing and admiration, and may new beginnings and new connections be manifested here, I earnestly ask and desire.

Father, please remember the many children scattered across the nation. Moreover, your beloved daughters are fighting on the front lines, shouldering a historic mission, so please do not let them think human thoughts even when they are lonely. Believing in your power that creates from nothing, and recalling your lonely life of restoration, may we have hearts that can praise with infinite glory when we find ourselves in a day and environment where we can do so, knowing that the connections of love will be established.

We must yearn for and love the nation on your behalf. As we face the reality of those eternally bound in the chains of the enemy within the realm of death, we must stand in a place where we forget our own prestige in our earnest desire to liberate them, knowing that the path of pioneering you have woven will be opened without reservation.

We must understand that in a place where we only think of ourselves, we can only grow distant from you. Please allow us to forget ourselves and feel you with our entire being.
276   In Search of Truth
When we believe and live with our whole being, a spring day of recreation comes to us.  
It is pitiful that Abel must love again the nation that betrayed us, and it is also pitiful that this group, bearing the responsibility of Abel, must go back to meet the established church members who drove us to the path of death and embrace them, weeping.  
Every time we stand in such a position, even if people do not recognize us, the angelic world in the spirit realm and the countless saints treat us with hundreds and thousands of times more earnest and heartfelt feelings. Therefore, even though we do not have a nation in this world, we must be grateful that the nation of the spirit world has become our nation. Even if we are mocked in front of the people of the world, we must give thanks for being welcomed in front of the prophets and our ancestors in heaven.  
While admiring the value of being responsible for this tremendous field that exists only for a moment in history, I find myself in such a miserable position, walking a pitiful path, becoming the focus of attention of many people, and weaving the fabric of daily life. During this granted period, may your grace overflow upon the children who are determined and sincere.  
As you have encouraged me on the path I have come, and as you have comforted me with your abundant love, I earnestly ask and desire that you grant such grace to them as well.  
May they forget the shameful desires of the sun and be equipped with the liberated daughter’s appearance who can pledge for tomorrow amid hope and aspirations, making them strong, brave, and steadfast before the nation, so that they can devote themselves wholeheartedly to fulfilling their entrusted responsibilities.  
You have said, "Love your God with all your heart, with all your soul, and with all your strength." There is a heart of the Father who wishes for us to love the nation and the world with all our heart, soul, and strength, so we must first establish a connection with the Father. Knowing the content of your command, we understand that those who forget themselves and love their nation passionately will not perish. May we become holy daughters who can dedicate a limited day in such a position as an offering of infinite value before the Father.  
As we are destined to speak in the future and to lead a meaningful life, we realize that it is the mission of today’s Unification Church that cannot be passed on to anyone else. I earnestly request that the Father directly oversee this position they are guarding, and quietly leave that connection eternally with them, and be with them forever. I sincerely ask and desire that the Father allows us to welcome the results of victory together with this pitiful group.  
I believe there are many who are praying towards this headquarters while considering their lonely circumstances at this time. With a heart greater than that, may we fulfill our responsibilities as priests before them, guard the altar, and be a sincere group eagerly awaiting the manifestation of heavenly glory.  
Please remember the many children scattered overseas, Father. May they not be ashamed before the kingdom of hope for tomorrow, and may they devote all their energy to fulfilling their national mission.  
Please take charge of this time, Father. On this holy day, as the year 1970 draws to a close, may abundant blessings rest upon those who have gathered to keep this day, and may you connect them in a way that allows them to boast of this day. I ask this once again, and I offer all these words in the name of True Parents. Amen.  
<Words> People often think centered around themselves. We often feel in our daily lives that anyone thinks and acts from a position where they recognize themselves as good and true.  
Humans who seek to relate to good things  
When something good happens, they want to take the lead, and even when something joyful occurs, they do the same. Or, when there is something of infinite value, it is human nature to want to establish a connection with it first. When we ask ourselves if we have become the ones who can possess that which we like, we find that no one can answer affirmatively.  
No matter how good the environment may be, before praising that good environment, we first think about how much that environment is related to us. In other words, we wish for that environment to be connected with us and to result in something with us. The better the environment, the more we want to connect with it, and the more eternal it is, the more we want to relate to it. Thus, we humans wish for our lives to be centered around our own individuality.  
In this light, we must ask ourselves how we have come to stand in such a position. What is the cause that leads us to boldly step forward and seek relationships without thinking or feeling boredom or criticism? This is because the heart knows that humans are meant to be in such a position. We must understand this.  
If there is something precious that exists only once in the world, we want to relate to it. If there are ten thousand people, all ten thousand want to relate to it, and if there are three billion people, all three billion want to relate to that one precious thing. This is human nature.  
Then, if three billion people long for that one thing and wish to be concentrated in its value, it follows that today’s three billion people must go through a path of struggle to possess that one thing. When we calmly look at our living environment, the issue arises that to possess this infinite value, we must struggle and win against thousands and tens of thousands of people, or even against all humanity. Today, we must reflect on whether our desire to connect with that one thing of the highest value is not contradictory.  
How to allow all people to share in that valuable thing is the question.  
If all people can equally possess such valuable things, what content can we use to connect with it? Can we relate to it as an infinite possession of mine, leaving it as an infinite connection to praise? Furthermore, how can we have an environment that can stimulate a more valuable content that can turn it not just into my own but into everyone’s? Today, the standard of desire centered around me and the good things of absolute value that I wish for differ in direction and position. Therefore, we are placed in a position where we must clarify one of these.  
Everyone wants to possess something of infinite value, and that desire is not a heart that wishes for oneself to become that, but it is undoubtedly a heart that all people have inherently. When we seek the path of value and face valuable content, there is a difference between the current environment we live in and the environment we will face in the future.  
If good things begin and end centered around me, and if joyful things also begin and end centered around me, then if there is something precious, true, and valuable in this universe, it would deny the participation of anyone else but me. If that is the case, we must conclude that the very desire of each of our hearts to seek the value of the whole centered around ourselves is contradictory.  
Then, what can elevate this to a universal and generally valuable content? Without determining this content from any standpoint, there is no solution. If fallen humans living on this earth pursue value centered around their physiology and ecology, they will enter into the most contradictory environment in history.  
Then, what is necessary for all people to equally possess that infinite value and inherit it as a standard of value? Since there is only one absolute value centered around our current selves, when I connect with that one and only value, I can praise it as the value of the whole without conflict, and at the same time as the value of the individual.  
Then, there must be a way, but what is that way? This is the question.  
When we think about this, you will find that today you are in a position where it is easy to forget yourself. The individual cannot be born independently, nor can it inherit. We must understand this. The existence of the individual is born and lives through the blood of parents, and even if someone claims that they can live for more than a century, they will inevitably meet the end of life within that century.  
However, human history must not end with a century; therefore, humans have the responsibility to extend this history. Thus, the issue of succession arises. In other words, the issue of inheritance and successors arises. Only when there is an heir who can inherit with a value that can shine brighter than myself can we go to the world of hope for tomorrow and the world of absolute value for tomorrow.  
However, if today’s self cannot pass on valuable content to the future and stands in a position of diminishing and sacrificing its own value, reality will reject him and block his path.  
Who can remain in the future world?  
Will the future world welcome someone who stands in a position where they consume the interests of the whole centered around themselves? Such a person will never be welcomed. It is only by leaving today’s valuable things for tomorrow that we can get closer to the future’s valuable things. To do this, how should we proceed? We must increase the value of tomorrow beyond today. That path becomes the decisive factor that can reach the world of absolute hope.  
Because humans are in such a fate, they unconsciously wish for goodness, admire good things, and long for valuable things. However, that which is valuable and good does not just relate to me as it is. There must be a price of sacrifice to connect. Bad things can connect without a price, but good things must be paid for with a price to connect. It is not just a price that flows away or is unnecessary for someone. In the historical process, one must pay a price that is necessary for everyone to connect and remain.  
Then, what becomes the necessary price for everyone? It is life itself. It is the irreplaceable vitality. What becomes the noble value pursued by the person who possesses that life? It is the counterpart. When we ask what can relate to that counterpart, the answer is only love. Only those who plant and invest the content of noble life and noble love can reach the absolute value of happiness for everyone in the future. We can conclude that there is no other way.  
The point of life  
Today, those who are good, who walk the path of goodness, who admire and pledge to the world connected to eternal and infinite absolute value, can invest their vitality for the future within their current living environment, and they can invest all their love for the future along with that life. Only then can the rights of inheritance of greater value expand. Therefore, when we see those who have pursued a new ideology with a purpose, they have spent their vitality and consumed all the elements of love they should have. We cannot deny that only such people have inherited and passed on history.  
Why is that? Because they have fallen. If humans had not fallen, the time of their birth would be spring, and the time of their growth would be summer. The rain would urge life, the shining sun would be the driving force to absorb the elements of life, and the blowing wind would be the environment promising a bright tomorrow. Everything that exists in such a good environment and is related to it does not present conflict to humans but promotes development.  
However, due to the fall of humans, we now find ourselves in such a miserable position where the consumption of our own selves has become necessary.  
When we see this, we realize that this consumption does not end as our own consumption but becomes a contribution to ourselves and a foundation for our own development and growth. Therefore, today, if we wish to relate to absolute goodness, we must pay the price of sacrifice. This is an unavoidable matter because we are entangled in the destiny of the fallen realm.  
If you wish to relate to good things and things of absolute value in your life journey, you should not praise and like your current self as it is. There is a desire of the heart to seek relationships and a desire of the body to seek relationships.  
If God did not create all things with an absolute purpose, then God cannot be absolute. Today, fallen humans also wish to create things that can achieve that purpose centered around God’s purpose. When we see this, the fact that within today’s humans there exist both body and mind pursuing different purposes is contradictory.  
As creations made by the absolute God, this should not be the case. Because God is one, the creations He made must also have one purpose. Among that one purpose, if humans are born with the title of God’s children, they should relate to that one purpose, and all should establish relationships centered around that purpose. Yet, why is there conflict between the closest body and mind within my individuality? This is because humans have fallen.  
Therefore, the point of purpose that life seeks, the one and only point of love that must eternally be together with life, can only be achieved within one purpose realm; it is impossible within two purpose realms. In such a place, the term absolute cannot be established. In a position that has relative rights within itself, one cannot find absolute value. This is the problem.  
Then, what should be the starting point in seeking absolute value today? We must seek the truth. If I clearly recognize the truth, cannot deny it, and wish for it to be continuously related to my life through the rising awareness or stimulation from my heart, then I must organize the position I am in now.  
Today, in the nation or world where you are born and live through your parents’ blood, you cannot find the truth as it is. To find the truth, you must set a certain limit and make a determination, whether it be a denial or affirmation. You must choose one. This is an unavoidable matter.  
The subject of goodness  
Here, some may ask whether the heart is good or the body is good. Or they may say that while one can deny the mind centered around the body, one cannot deny the body centered around the mind.  
Then let us think universally. Did I do well or not?
When looking at the problem, whether or not one feels a pang of conscience, whether or not there is shame in the heart, is something that you cannot deny you can feel when you ask yourself. 
When I say I do not feel a pang of conscience, I am confident. No matter what the world says, I will not bend. Even if the most threatening being in the universe, unique in its existence, directly confronts me, I will not yield. When there is no pang of conscience, one is infinitely strong. 
How far can that infinite limit go? Can I say "yes" when a central figure in the Republic of Korea denies it? No. Even if a central figure in the world denies it, I cannot say "yes." Furthermore, even if the central being of heaven and earth denies it, I cannot say "yes." No matter how much they try, I will say "no." If there is someone greater than God, I would still stand confidently before that being. That authority is absolute. 
If the heart has not done wrong, then no matter what my father, teacher, or anyone else says, I will not bend. I want to eradicate such people. After going against that, I would call them "these guys." My father would be one of those guys, and my teacher would be one of those guys. Everyone wants to win. That is how the heart is. 
When looking at this, it seems that there is no one in a pure position who does not feel a pang of conscience, but there is an absolute authority inherent in that position. Then, what value is this inherent authority seeking? It will seek absolute value. However, if we do not have the foundation to have such a story, we cannot pursue such an object. When asking whether that foundation is in my body or my heart, it turns out that the body cannot be the foundation. Therefore, what is the center? It is the heart. 
When we say someone is a good friend, it is because they are conscientious. Right? Is there anyone who says they like their friend because they are beautiful or handsome? It is because they are conscientious, pure, and self-sacrificing that they are liked. 
Therefore, what is the foundation for saying something is good, or what is its content? It is said to be good because it is pure, honest, without deceit, and self-sacrificing. Is there anyone who says they like someone because they are arrogant, self-serving, coercive, and individualistic? It is said to be good because they willingly accept any sacrifice for their friend. 
When thinking about this, in fact, people do not need education. All the liberal arts and such in universities are unnecessary. We all know it. Because we have a conscience, when we do something bad, we feel a pang of conscience saying, "Hey, why are you doing something bad?" Is there any education beyond that? Originally, education is unnecessary. That is why the problem is not solved at the end of the world, but it is solved from here. There are 100% solutions that can be resolved within your living sphere, and you all know that. 
Humans who want to leave good things and inherit them 
Then how do we want good things? Is there anyone who wants to throw away good things and leave bad things? Such a person can be caught and punished. They are dreadful. No matter how ugly it is, is there anyone who says, "I should throw away the good and leave the bad"? There is not. Therefore, good things remain forever. The conclusion comes naturally. 
The eternal is not somewhere else. Good things remain forever. Our hearts are just like that. Our hearts want to leave behind better things if there are better things. Then, who do we want to leave this to? We want to leave it to our beloved children. What does that child want to do? They also want to leave it to their beloved children. When that child comes to dominate the world, it becomes a global treasure. Just like that, we humans want to leave the best things behind. 
When asking what the best thing is, if someone says, "It is a lump of gold," they would want to leave that behind. However, there is something better than a lump of gold. What is it? It is a living being centered on love. Then, when asking what a living being centered on love is for me, that relationship is the most precious. 
When looking from the perspective of "me," where did "I" come from? I am not someone who just flew in. There are parents, which is why there are children. Parents symbolize the past, I symbolize the present, and children symbolize the future. Who is the decisive factor that brings together and connects the past, present, and future, which meet at a single point? It is today's "me." I cannot come into existence without the past, nor can I continue to exist without the future. That is why today, everyone wants to inherit historical value. 
If there are good antiques in the Republic of Korea, they want to make them their own. Then, who does the National Treasure No. 1, Namdaemun, belong to? It belongs to the Republic of Korea. What is the Republic of Korea's is also mine; it may not feel real, but it is mine. If I were to live alone in the Republic of Korea, it would feel real that it is mine. 
Then, from whom does the National Treasure No. 1, Namdaemun, start? It starts from me alone. If the Republic of Korea is "me," then that national treasure is both the Republic of Korea's and mine. Even in managing it, it would be nice if I could manage it alone, but since thirty million people manage it, I dislike that. However, one cannot manage it alone. Can one manage the entire national treasure by oneself? It must be managed cooperatively by all. Good things must be managed that way. 
Greater than parental love is God's love 
When there is something good, one wants to boast about it. Right? One wants to advertise it. What does wanting to advertise mean? It means wanting to establish a relationship. The reason for advertising or boasting is to say, "You should also establish a relationship like this." What is the best thing for a person? The best is parents, then oneself, and then children. This is how history is inherited. What is the essence of this content? It is the foundation where our lives are connected and where the environment connected to life can blossom with love. This is the family. 
When looking at the family, the child says, "Mother is eternally mine." The mother is happy to share her blood with the child. When looking at this, what is good? It is sacrificing for others. The reason a friend is good is also because of sacrifice. It is said to be good because one is happy to give to others. What is liked is wanting to give the most precious thing to oneself while sacrificing for others. It is not about giving and then wanting to take it back, but rather giving while feeling ashamed that it is too little. That is parental love. 
However, a child's love is not like that. That is why parental love and children's love are different. Parents feel regret for not being able to give something better while giving, and children think they are satisfied by saying, "I am a filial child." Thus, parental love and children's love are different. They say, "I did this, but what did mom and dad do?" A child's love has limits. It cannot go beyond the boundary of self. However, parental love transcends the boundary of self. 
What kind of love is this? This love is God's love. The content of God's love manifested before humanity is parental love. 
Then, what kind of being is God? When thinking about it centered on parents, God must be greater. Our parents love only their children, but God loves all humanity just as a parent loves their child. Do you understand what I mean? The mother and father who gave birth to me love only me, but God is in a position that loves all people as a mother and father. 
Then, what kind of being is God? He is a being who constantly has a heart that wants to give more and more, even after giving for a thousand years. Because He is such a being, we seek God; if God were a merchant who says, "Hey, this is worth this much," then we do not need such a God. 
Why should all people like and follow God? When looking at the question of why we should like God, it is because God gives everything for all people and, while giving, feels ashamed, saying, "Right now, this is all I can give, but just wait a little longer; I will give you something a hundredfold, a thousandfold better..." He is not satisfied with what He gives in the present but has the heart to promise to give something better in the future. That is why being with such a being is happiness, even if one cannot eat or live. If one enters a place of hunger, the stimulus of hope for the future is felt shockingly within the realm of reality. What does this mean? It means that one can make a new resolution. 
In a position of giving while feeling ashamed, if a child with such parents calls out, "Mom!" will they just hug their body? How grateful they would be! That position is one where tears of comfort can be shed together for the future. It is not despairing together, but rather seeing tomorrow's hope as a stimulus in the present, resolving together, and being able to encourage each other in an explosive way. 
Therefore, the phenomenon that appears there is not miserable. It is only in that love realm that one can draw in the stimulus for the future and praise the value within the realm of reality. That is why it concludes that those who live in that love realm have no unhappiness. Do you understand what I mean? 
A person who can reap 
Then, Jesus came to fulfill the messianic mission before all people; what kind of being is that? It is not a petty messiah that we do not want. If one's own parents cannot be messiahs, then we do not need a messiah who is inferior to them. He must be greater than parents. He must be good. What is good? It must be able to sacrifice one's life and wish for blessings for a thousand years. If that is not the case, one cannot be the messiah of all people. Because He had such content, just before Jesus died on the cross, He cried with tears for His enemies, saying, "Forgive their sins." This cannot be done by anyone who is not a parent. 
No matter how much a child may be a scoundrel, a child who must disappear like dew on the gallows, the heart of a parent wants to forgive a thousand times. There is nothing that cannot be forgiven between parents and children. Even a scoundrel child has the way to repent and be reborn in despair. It is because of the laws of the state, but between parents and children, there is nothing that cannot be forgiven. 
If this has become a tradition, then a child who has grown up knowing such love within that love realm cannot be unfilial. It is absolutely impossible to be unfilial. A child who has grown up in the embrace of parents with such love cannot be unfilial before their parents, nor can siblings fail to harmonize. 
Then, what is a truly true person? As mentioned earlier, it is a person who sacrifices and serves. It is a person who can rejoice even when seeing their current self being consumed. 
The consumed self does not end in consumption but can become the motive for future harvest. Therefore, planting does not lead to destruction but to prosperity. Such a person is one who can reap. 
To do that, one must throw oneself away. One must plant oneself. One must plant purely. Planting itself becomes a sacrifice. That itself is the seed falling. It is self-denial. If one can smoothly deny oneself, then a new life force of affirmation will arise, becoming the motive for promising tomorrow's harvest. 
Therefore, a good person is not someone who is self-centered. Right? This is absolute. It is not about being self-centered. A good person is someone who is centered on the whole. Then, where is the limit of that whole? Is it the Republic of Korea? It goes far beyond the Republic of Korea. Is it global? It goes far beyond the world. That is why the world of religion has emerged. 
A good person is a person who sacrifices 
What kind of people are thinkers, great figures, or saints? If today in the Republic of Korea, someone says, "Oh, all people! Listen to our country's claims," they may have founded a nationalistic country, but they cannot contribute to the world. Those who claim to have joined the ranks of saints are at least those who have made claims with a global content. Without such a person, one cannot become a saint.
